Me tiri yɛɛ yie biribiara anto me, nanso mehunu adeɛ a ɛyɛ hu pa ara wɔ m’ani so, wɔ berɛ a na nkurɔfoɔ rebɔ wɔn ho mmɔden sɛ wɔbɛpae nhwehwɛ afa mu apue.
Na ebinom de nkonnwa rebobɔ mpoma no ano, nanso na mpoma no ntumi mmubu.
"Mpoma no baako ho buuiɛ maa wɔhyɛɛ aseɛ sɛ wɔbɛfa mu apue," wei ne nsɛm a Franciszek Kowal a ɔnyaa ne tiri didiim kaeɛ.
Nsroma ma yɛn kanea ne ɔhyew esiane ahoɔden a ɛda adi wɔ aberɛ a ‘hydrogen atoms’ adi afra (anaa ahyiam) redane ‘element’ a emu yɛ duru.
Abɔdeɛ mu nyansapɛfoɔ reyɛ adwumaden a ɛbɛboa ama wɔatumi ayɛ adeɛ a ɛno nso bɛtumi ama anyinam ahoɔden.
Wei yɛ ɔhaw kɛseɛ a ne ko yɛ den pa ara na ɛbɛtumi adi mfeɛ bebree ansa na wɔatumi ayɛ deɛ ɛbɛdi dwuma yie.
Dadeɛ a yɛakontono no nante nsuo ani esiane nsuo ani bɔberɛ nti.
Nsuo ani bɔberɛ no yɛ adwuma firisɛ, ‘molecules’ a ɛwɔ nsuo no ani no ka bom deɛ emu yɛ den sene mframa ‘molecules’ no a ɛwɔ nsuo no so no.
Nsuo ‘molecules’ no yɛ honam ani adeɛ a ɛwɔ nsuo ani, na ɛma kwan ma nneɛma bi te sɛ nnadeɛ tumi nante nsuo ani.
Dadebena a ɛda ‘skate’ a wɔtwi no sukɔkyea soɔ no wɔ afaafa mmienu a emu ayɛ donko. Afaa mmienu no boa ma ɛtumi kyere asukɔkyea no, wɔ berɛ akyea mu.
Esiane sɛ dadebena no ase akoa nti, sɛ dadeɛ no kyea kɔ afa ne afa a, n’afa a ɛne asukɔkyea no nya nkutaho no so kyea.
Wei na ɛboa ne ɔretwi no ma no twa ne ho. Sɛ ‘skate’ no kyea kɔ nifa a, deɛ ɔretwie no nso kɔ nifa, sɛ ɛkɔ benkum nso a, deɛ ɔretwie no nso kɔ benkum.
Sɛ ɛbɛtumi asane anya ahoɔden dada a na ɛwɔ no a, gye sɛ wɔgyae ahoɔden a watwe afiri kanea mu no.
Wɔyɛ saa wɔ berɛ wɔreyiyi nkanea nketenkete bi adi a wɔfrɛ no "photon".
Abɔdeɛ mu nyansapɛfoɔ frɛɛ dwumadie yi "stimulated emission of radiation" ɛfiri sɛ ‘atoms’ no nya ahoɔden firi nkanea a ɛhyerɛn mu, na ama ‘photon of light’ nso apue, ɛna kanea nso yɛ ‘radiation’ no fa bi.
Mfonii a ɛtoa so no kyerɛ sɛnea ‘atoms’ da ‘photons’ adi. Ampa, nokorɛ mu no ‘photons’ susua sene nea ɛwɔ mfonii yi mu.
‘photons’ mpo susua sene nneɛma ɛka bom bɛdane ‘atoms’ mpo.
Nnɔnhwere ɔha akyi a wɔyɛɛ ho adwuma no, ahoma tea a ɛhyɛ kanea no mu no hyeeɛ na kanea no antumi anyɛ adwuma bio.
Ɛba saa a na ɛhia sɛ yɛsesa kanea no. Ɛwɔ sɛ yɛyɛahwɛyie yɔ berɛ a yɛresesa kanea.
Deɛ ɛi kan, ɛwɔ sɛ yɛdum adeɛ a yɛde sɔ kanea no anaa yɛtwe anyinam kanea n’ahoma no firim.
Sɛnti ne sɛ, anyinam ahoɔden a ɛnam bea a yɛde sɔ kanea no a ɛyɛ dadeɛ a ɛwɔ kanea no ho no bɛtumi ama ogya afa yɛn mu wɔ berɛ a yɛn nsa akɔka saa dadeɛ no, anaa sɛ yɛn nsa akɔka dadeɛ no wɔ berɛ ɛho kakra aka bea a yɛde hyɛ mu no.
Akwaa no mu deԑ ԑhia pa ara ‘aforo sane die wɔ nnipadua’ no mu ne akoma, ԑno na ԑpu mogya gu nnipadua no mu.
Mogya firi akoma no mu fa dorobԑn bi a yԑfrԑ no ‘arteries’ mu kɔ na asane afa dorobԑn a yԑfrԑ no ‘veins’ mu aba akoma no mu. Dorobԑn nketewa pa ara no din de ‘capillaries’.
‘Triceratop’ se ntumi nwe nwura nko ara na mmom ԑtumi we dua mman ne nhini a ԑyԑ den pa ara.
Abɔdeԑ mu nyansapԑfoɔ bi dwene sԑ ‘Triceratops’ di ‘cycads’, a ԑyԑ dua bi a na ԑnyԑ nna wɔ Cretaceous.
Saa dua yi te sԑ abԑ dua ԑnna ԑwɔ nhaban a ano no yԑ feafea.
Nka ‘Triceratops’ bԑtumi de n’ano denden no ayi ahaban no ansa na awe dua no ankasa.
Abɔdeԑ mu nyansapԑfoɔ no bi nso se saa dua yi wɔ awuduro ԑno nti ԑnyԑ adeԑ a ‘dinosaur’ biara di, ԑwom sԑ seisei ‘sloth’ ԑne mmoa bi te sԑ ako (a wɔfiri dinosaurs no ase) no tumi di nhaban anaa nnuaba a awuduro wom.
Ɛbԑyԑ dԑn na ahoɔden a ԑwɔ Io atumi atwe me? Sԑ wogyina Io ani a, wo mu duru a wowɔ no Asase so no so te.
Obi a ne mu duru yԑ 200 pounds (90kg) wɔ Asase so no mu duru wɔ Io no bԑyԑ 36 pounds (16kg). Ɛno nti ahoɔden no bԑtwe wo kakra.
Awia no nni ‘crust’ a wobԑtumi agyina so te sԑ Asase deԑ no. Awia no nyinaa yԑ ‘egyaframa’, egya, ne ‘plasma’.
Mmerԑ dodoɔ a woretwe wo ho firi awia no ho no na ‘egyaframa’ no mu reyԑ ha.
Sԑ yԑhwԑ awia no a, akyire no a yԑhunu no de ‘photosphere’, a ԑkyerԑ sԑ, "kanea kurukuruwa".
Mfeԑ mpem mmiԑnsa akyi no, afe 1610 mu no, ‘Italian astronomer Galileo Galilei’ de ‘telescope’ hunuu sԑ, Venus wɔ nkyekyԑmu bi te sԑ deԑ bosome wɔ no.
Saa nkyekyԑmu yi ba ԑfiri sԑ Venus (anaa Bosome) no fa a ԑkyerԑ Awia no nko ara na ԑnya kanea. Venus nkyekyԑmu yi kaa bi too ‘Copernicus adwenkyerԑ’ so sԑ ‘planets’ no twa Awia ho hyia.
Mfeԑ kakra bi akyire 1639 no, ‘English astronomer a ɔde Jeremiah Horrocks’ hunuu sԑ Venus firi baabi kɔ baabi.
Na England san dii Danelaw so nkonim no, onyaa asomdwoe pii bere tenten.
Nanso, wɔ afe 991 mu no Ethelred hyiaa Viking a na ne dɔm no dɔɔso paa kyɛn dɔm biara no, efiri Guthrum deɛ no so, bɛyɛ mfe apem a na aba kɔ no.
Nea na odi saa dɔm no anim ne Olaf Trygvasson, Norwayni a na ne botae ne sɛ ɔbɛgye ne man afiri Danefo no nnisoɔ ase.
Wɔ asraafo no nkuguo a edi kan no akyi no, Ethelred tumi ne Olaf yɛɛ nhehyɛe, na ɔsan kɔɔ Norway kɔbɔɔ mmɔden sɛ ne nsa bɛka n'ahinni no. Ɛyɛɛ te sɛ nkunim ne nkuguo a adi afrafra.
Hangeul nko ara ne atwerԑdeԑ a wɔde baeԑ a wɔde di dwuma da biara. Saa atwerԑdeԑ yi bae wɔafe 1444 mu Ɔhene Sejong ahennie berԑ so (1418 – 1450).
Na Ɔhene Sejong yԑ ɔhene a ɔtɔ so nnan wɔ Joseon Dynasty no mu ԑnna ɔyԑ obi a wɔbu no pa ara.
Ɔdii kan too Hangeul atwerԑdeԑ no din Hunmin Jeongeum, a ԑkyerԑ sԑ "nnyegyeeԑ pa no a yԑde tenetene ɔmanfoɔ no".
Adwenkyerԑ bebree wɔ hɔ fa kwan a Sanskrit faa so baeԑ ho. Wɔn mu baako fa ‘Aryan akwantuo’ a wɔde firi atɔeԑ wuraa India mu a na wɔde wɔn kasa nam ho.
Sanskrit yԑ tete kasa na yԑbԑtumi de atoto Latin kasa a wɔka no wɔ Europe no ho.
Tete nwoma a na ԑwɔ wiase no nyinaa na wɔatwerԑ no Sanskrit kasa mu. Wɔkekaa ‘Upanishads’ sii ani wieeԑ no, Sanskrit yerae ԑnam tumi nnidisoɔ nti.
Sanskrit yԑ kasa a ԑyԑ den na ԑyԑ dԑ a ԑno ne India kasa bebree farebae, sԑdeԑ Latin nso yԑ Europe kasa bi te sԑ French ne Spanish farebae no.
Berԑ a wɔne France ntɔkwa no baa awieeԑ no, Germany yԑԑ ahoboa sԑ wɔbԑto ahyԑ Britain so.
Germany too saa ɔsa yi din “Operation Sealion”. Britain asogyafoɔ no akodeԑ bebree yerae berԑ a wɔtu firii Dunkirk no nti na wɔayԑ mmrԑ.
Nanso na Roya Navy no da so wɔ ahoɔden sene German Navy no (“Kriegsmarine”) a sԑ obiara bԑto hyԑԑ English Channel no so a, anka wɔbԑdi ne so nkonim.
Nanso na Roya Navy no suhyԑn no kakra bi na na ԑwɔ baabi a atamfo no bԑfa aba ԑfiri sԑ na akannifoɔ no suro sԑ German de akodeԑ firi soro bԑha wɔn.
Ma yԑnhyԑ aseԑ mfiri Italy nhyehyԑeԑ no nkyerԑmu no ho. Na Italy yԑ Germany ne Japan "nuabarima ketewa".
Na wɔn asogyafoɔ ne navy no nni ahoɔden, ԑwom sԑ na wɔayԑ suhyԑn mono nnan ansa naɔ ko no rehyԑ aseԑ.
Na deԑ Italy repԑ nyinaa ne Afrika aman. Sԑ wɔbԑtumi anya saa aman yi a, na wɔhia sԑ wɔnya akofoɔ a wɔbԑfa ԑpo no so saa de abԑwura Afrika.
Ɛno nti, na ԑsԑ sԑ wɔyi baabi a Britain wɔ ne wɔn suhyԑn a ԑwɔ Egypt no nyinaa firi hɔ. Sԑ wɔyi saa adeԑ yi to nkyԑn a, na ԑnni sԑ Italy akofoɔ no yԑ biribi foforɔ biara.
Afei Japan. Na asuo atwa Japan ho ahyia te sԑ Britain.
‘Submarines’ yԑ suhyԑn a wɔayԑ sԑ ԑmfa asuo ase, na ԑnwɔ hɔ berԑ bi mu.
Wɔde ‘Submarines’ dii dwuma wɔ Wiase Ntɔkwa kɛseɛ I ԑne Wiase Ntɔkwa kɛseɛ II’ no mu. Saa berԑ no na ԑyԑ nyaa ԑnna ԑsane nso wɔ baabi pɔtee a ԑtumi to tuo kɔduru.
Ɔko no ahyԑaseԑ no na wɔtaa fa asuo no ani, nanso berԑ rekɔ n’anim no ‘submarines’ no kɔɔ asuo no ase sԑdeԑ ԑbԑyԑ a wɔnhu wɔn.
Na wɔfrԑ German ‘submarines’ no U-Boats. Na Germanfoɔ no ayԑ adeԑ wɔ kwan a wɔfa so de ‘submarines’ di dwuma no ho.
Ɛnam kwan a na wɔfa so de ‘submarines’ no di dwuma yie no nti, ɔko no akyi no wɔannye Germanfoɔ no anni sԑ wɔwɔ bebree.
Aane! Ɔhene Tutankhamun, a ԑtɔ da a wɔtumi frԑ no "King Tut" anaa "The Boy King", yԑ tete Egypt ahemfo no mu baako a wɔnim no berԑ yi mu.
Deԑ ԑyԑ nwanwa ne sԑ na wɔnhu no sԑ ne ho hia tete mmerԑ no mu nti wɔantwerԑ ne ho asԑm tete ahemfo nwoma bebree mu.
Nanso berԑ a wɔhuu ne nna afe 1922 mu no ԑmaa nnipa huu no yie. Akorɔmfoɔ wiaa nna bebree mu adeԑ nanso ne deԑ no nko ara deԑ, wɔamfa wɔn nsa anka.
Na nneԑma a wɔde siee Tutankhamun no bebree a wɔhɔ a ԑnyԑԑ hwee, a nneԑma a wɔde sika kɔkɔɔ ne aboɔ a ԑho hia ayԑ mpempem ka ho.
‘Spoke wheels’ a Assyriafoɔ no yԑeԑ no maa wɔn apɔnkɔ no mu yԑԑ ha sane ho yԑԑ hare a na wɔbԑtumi asane asogyafoɔ ne apɔnkɔfoforɔ ho.
Na wɔn pea no tumi wura asogyafoɔ a wɔne wɔn reko no akokyԑm no mu. Bԑyԑ 1000 B.C., Assyriafoɔ de ‘cavalry’ a ԑdi kan no baeԑ.
‘Cavalry’ yԑ asogyafoɔ a wɔtena apɔnkɔ akyi di ako. Saa berԑ no na wɔnyԑԑ ‘deԑ wɔde gu pɔnkɔ akyi’ no nti na wɔtena apɔnkɔ no akyi saa ara na wɔdi ako no.
Yԑnim Greek amanyɔfoɔ, abɔdeԑ mu paadehunufoɔ, mfoninyԑfoɔ bebree. Ebia wɔn mu deԑ yԑnim no pa ara ne Homer, onifrani a na ɔka anwonsԑm no a ɔyԑԑ Greek kasadwini mmienu: ‘the poems Iliad ԑne Odyssey’ no.
‘Sophocles ԑne Aristophanes’ yԑ wɔn a wɔtwerԑ ahwԑgorɔ nwoma a wɔwɔ din pa ara na wɔn ahwԑgorɔ ka wiase kasadwini a ԑdi mu pa ara no ho bi.
Greekni a wagye din bio yԑ ‘mathematician Pythagoras’, a dodoɔ no ara nim no sԑ ɔde ayɔnkofa a ԑda ‘triangle’ afaafa no ntam no baeԑ no.
Nnipa dodoɔ a wɔka Hindi no sesa. Wɔkyerԑ sԑ ԑyԑ ԑfiri mmienu kɔsi nnan mu kasa a nnipa dodoɔ ka pa ara wɔ wiase.
Nnipa dodoɔ a wɔfiri kuro no mu ka kasa no sesa a ne nnyinasoɔ no yԑ nkorabata a wɔkan no.
Nnipa dodoɔ a wɔde wɔn ani bu sԑ wɔka kasa no yԑ bԑyԑ ɔpepem 340 kɔsi ɔpepem 500, ԑnna wɔn a wɔte no yԑ ɔpepem 800.
Hindi ԑne Urdu sԑ wɔn sԑmfua a ԑde di dwuma mu nanso atwerԑ mu deԑ, ԑsesa; nnipa a wɔka kasa no mmienu bԑtumi ate wɔn ho ase wɔ daadaa nkɔmmɔdie mu.
Mfeɛ ɔha a ɛtɔ so 15th mu hɔ no, na ‘Estonia Atifi fam’ hyԑ Germany amanneԑ ase.
Na Germanfoɔ bi pԑ sԑ wɔka Onyankopɔn ho asԑm kyerԑ nnipa no, ԑno nti wɔyԑԑ ‘Estonian literal language’ no.
Na ne nnyinasoɔ yԑ German atwerԑdeԑ no ԑnna wɔde atwerԑdeԑ baako yi "Õ/õ" kaa ho.
Mmerԑ bi akyi no nsԑmfua bebree a wɔfԑm firii German kasa mu bԑnyaa nteaseԑ. Wei ne anibue ahyԑaseԑ.
Amammerԑ kwan so no, deԑ ɔbԑdi adeԑ no wura sogya mu berԑ a wawie sukuu no.
Nanso, Charles kɔɔ suapɔn wɔTrinity College, Cambridge ԑhɔ na ɔsuaa ‘Anthropology ԑne Archaeology’, ԑne ‘History’ akyire yi, a ɔnyaa 2:2 (suapɔn abodin a yɛfrɛ no).
Charles ne onipa a ɔdi kan wɔ Britania Adehye Abusua no mu a ɔnyaa abodin krataa.
'European Turkey (eastern Thrace or Rumelia in the Balkan peninsula) yԑ ɔman no mu 3%.
Turkey ano bԑboro 1,600 kilometres (1,000 mi) wɔ ne tenten mu ԑne 800 km (500 mi) wɔ ne tԑtrԑtԑ mu, akɔyԑ ‘rectangular shape’.
Turkey beaeԑ no wɔ weinom ka ho ‘lakes, ԑfa 783,562 square kilometres (300,948 sq mi), a emu 755,688 square kilometres (291,773 sq mi) wɔ Asia anaafoɔ atɔeԑ ԑnna 23,764 square kilometres (9,174 sq mi) wɔ Europe’.
Turkey beaeԑ no ma no yԑ wiase mu ɔman a ԑtɔ so 37 a ԑso pa ara, ԑnna ԑreyԑ ne ‘Metropolitan France ԑne the United Kingdom’ a yԑaka abom ayԑ pԑ.
Ɛpo atwa Turkey ho ahyia wɔ baabi mmiԑnsa: ‘Aegean Sea no wɔ atɔeԑ, Black Sea no wɔ atifi ԑnna Mediterranean Sea no wɔ anaafoɔ.
Luxembourg wↄ abakↄsεm tenten nanso wↄn ahofadie afe a efi 1839 nka ho.
Na εnnε bere wei mu Belgiunm fa bi ka Luxembourg ho tete no nanso εbεyε sε Belgium wↄ 1830 Belgian Revolution.
Luxembourg man no bↄ wↄn ho mmↄden sε wↄnngyina ↄfa biara nanso Germany man no mu wↄde wↄn ho hyε Wiase Nyinaa Ko I ne Wiase Nyinaa Ko II no mu.
Wↄ afe 1957 mu no, Luxemburg bεyεε aman a wↄtee kuo bi a εnnε wↄfrε no European Union.
Drukgyal Dzong yε abankεseε a adane dantuo na esane yↄ Buddahfoↄ ahotefoↄ efie a εwↄ Paro ↄmansini no atififam (wↄ Phondey Akuraseε).
Wↄka sε wↄ afe 1649 mu no, Zhabdrung Ngaawang Namgyel yε abankεseε no maa nkonim a odii wↄ Tibetan_mongol asrafoↄ so no.
Wↄ afe 1951 mu no, ogyahyehyε bi siia nnoↄma nyinaa hyeeε nanso tete Drukgyal Zhabdrung Ngawang nnoↄma no kaa yε, ebi yε Zhabdrung Ngawang Namgyal ahoni no.
Ogyahyehyε no akyi no, wↄ koraa abankεseε no so na wↄbↄↄ ho ban nso, εno ma no bεyεε Bhutan ade a εtwetwe amanfoↄ na εmaa wↄn ahomeka.
Wↄ mfe mpem ahawↄtwe bere mu no Cambodia man no bεhyε aman mmienu a wↄwↄ tumi paa ntamu, Thailand ne Vietnam.
Thailandfoↄ no to hyε Cambodia man no so mpεn pii wↄ mfe mmpem ahawↄtwe bere no mu na 1772 mu no wↄ sεe Phom Phen.
Wↄ mfe a etwa toↄ wↄ mfe mpem ahawↄtwe bere mu no Vietnamfoↄ no nso to hyεε Cambodia so.
Venezuelafoↄ ↄha mu nkekyemu duowↄtwe na wↄn nyε adwuma, na wↄn a wↄyε adwuma no nso yε nnwuma a εnhyε aban aseε.
Venezuelafoↄ mu mmienu mu nkekyemu mmiεnsa a wↄyε adwuma no yε ↄsom adwuma, bεyε nkyeyemu anan yε adwuma wↄ adwumayε beaε a wↄ danedane asase so nnoↄma ani na nkyeyemu anum yε kuayↄ adwuma.
Asase so nnoↄma a εsomboↄ paa ma Venezuelafoↄ no yε ngo, na ↄman no de emufa kεseε tu kwan kↄ nkuro foforↄ so, emfa ho sε wↄn mu ↄha mu nkekyemu baako pε na εyↄ adwuma wↄ ngo ho adwumayε beaε hↄ.
Wↄ ↄman no ahofadie mfiaseε no, Singapore Botanic turo ho nimdiefoↄ boa ma wↄ sesaa nsuopↄw no bεyεε no Garden City asase a εhye wↄ so.
Wↄ afe 1981 no wↄ faa, Vanda Miss Joaquim, orchid nhwiren, sε ↄman no nhwiren.
Afe biara no wↄ Ahinime mu no mmoa a wↄwe ahaban ↄpepem baako ne aha num tu kↄ anaafoↄ asase pradadaa so, na wↄtwa Mara Asubↄnten, firi atififam bepↄ so nsuo no enti.
Na wↄnam atↄeεfam san ba atififam, na wↄ san twa Mara asubↄnten no ba, nsuo tↄ no akyiri wↄ Oforisuo mu.
Serengeti man no mmoa tenabea wↄ Serengeti mantemu, mmoa tenabea a εwↄ Ngorongoro ne Maswa mmoa tenabea a εwↄ Tanzania ne Maasai Mara man no mmoa tenabea wↄ Kenya.
Dawurubↄ mu nkotahodie ho adesua hwehwε sε wotumi nya nkↄmmↄ ne amammerε ho nimdeε, saa nso na εsε sε wonya nnwinade a wosua wↄ adesuadan mu no nso ho nimdeε paa (anansesεm a wↄkyerεw wↄ kyerεwpon so, ↄbↄtie ne ↄhwεtie mu nyiyimu, anasesεm ka, ne neaε εkeka ho.)
Nkↄmmↄbↄ ho bↄtirimuyε hwehwε sε wo san susu dea wodwene fa dawurubↄ adwuma ho na wosua sε wobεdwene nnoↄma ho wↄ akwan ahodoↄ so.
Nkↄmmↄbↄ ho bↄtirimyε hwehwε sε nhyehyεeε ho nnoↄma nyinaa hyia, nanso εsε sε ne nyinaa yε adeε a nyansa wↄ mu sε woyiyi no baako baako a.
Ↄhaw a εwↄ zoom mfoninitwa nhwehwε ho yε ne focal ho adwuma a εyε bisibasa ne mfoninitwa ahwehwε ho nnoↄma a εho hia na watumi anya focal ntwemu a εwↄ anim sen mfoninitwa nhwehwε a εba fam deε.
Saa ↄhaw wei abεyε ↄhaw ketewa ama wↄn a wↄyε mfoninitwa ahwehwε efiri sε wↄtumi yε mfoninitwa ahwehwε a εyε papa.
Wei ama zoom mfoninitwa ahwehwε no tumi ma mfonini yεfε paa te sε dea wↄde mfoninitwa ahwehwε a εwↄ focal ntwemu pↄtee na etwaaeε.
Ↄhaw foforↄ a εwↄ zoom mfonintwa nhwehwε ho ne sε akwan a kanea famu (ahoↄhareε) no εtae wↄ fam.
Wei ma no yε den sε wode zoom mfoninitwa nhwehwε a ne bo wↄ fam no betwa mfonini wↄ beaε a kanea nni anaa kanea εwↄ fam.
Ɔhaw baako a wɔtaa hyia bere a wode sini rekɔ DVD so no ne sɛ mfoni no fa bi kɔtɛ nkyɛn bere a worebɔ no.
TV ahodoɔ pii wɔ hɔ a wɔyɛ de sɔ ɔmanfoɔ pii no ani.
Eno nti, biribiara a wohu wɔ TV so no wɔ ɛhyeɛ a atwa wɔ soro, fam, ne nkyɛn nkyɛn.
Wɔyɛ saa de ma mfoni no nyinaa kata anim. Brɔfo kasa mu no wɔfrɛ no "overscan", a ase kyerɛ sɛ mfoni no bi kɔtɛ ɛfa bere a worebɔ no.
Nanso, sɛ woyɛ DVD a, ebia wobetwa ne hyeɛ nso. Na sɛ sini no wɔ nkyrɔeɛ a ɛbɛn aseɛ hɔ pii a, ne nyinaa ɛmma yiye.

Mysticism ɛyɛ hu a obi behu twaka a ɛda obi ne adeɛ bi ntam, hu a obehu ne ho ne adeɛ bi, anaa sɛ obi be hu dea ɛwɔ hɔ ankasa, sɛdeɛ biribi kyɛn so, honhom ho nokware, anaa Onyankopɔn.
Ɔgyedini no hwԑ sԑ ɔbԑnya suahunu anaa nhunumu wɔ nyame bi/bosom bi mu.
Akyidifoɔ no bɔ wɔn bra kwan bi so anaa nneԑma bi a ԑma saa suahunu no kɔ nkan.
Deԑ ԑma ‘Mysticism’ da nso firi ԑsom foforɔ ho ne suahunu a wɔsi so dua sԑ obi nya wɔ berԑ a ɔde n’adwene asi so ne titire ne asomdwoeԑ, nhunumu, nhyira anaa anigyeԑ mmorosoɔ so no.
‘Sikhism’ yԑ som a ԑfiri ‘India’. Ɛhyԑԑ aseԑ firii ‘Punjab’ mpɔtam hɔ wɔ ‘15th mfeɛ ɔha a ɛtɔ so berԑ no mu wɔ berԑ a nkyekyԑmu baa ‘Hindu amammerԑ’ mu no.
‘Sikhs’ no hunu wɔn som no sԑ ԑne ‘Hinduism’ no nyԑ pԑ ԑwom sԑ wɔgye tom sԑ ԑfiri ‘Hindu amammerԑ’ mu na ԑbaeԑ.
‘Sikhs’ no frԑ wɔn som no ‘Gurmat’ a ԑyԑ Punjabi ma "guru no akwan". ‘Guru’ no yԑ India som no nyinaa fapem nanso ‘Sikhism’ mu no, ayԑ ade titire a ԑyԑ ‘Sikh’ gyedie nnyinasoɔ.
Guru Nanak (1469–1539) na ɔtee saa som yi wɔ ‘15th mfeɛ ɔha a ɛtɔ so no mu. Ɔno akyi no, ‘guru’ ahodoɔ nkron na aba.
Nanso Ayԑwohomumu 1956 mu no, basabasayԑ a ԑmaa ne ho so wɔ Poland sɔɔ Krushchev bɔhyԑ no hwԑeԑ, wɔ berԑ a na adwumayԑfoɔ a wɔreyԑ ɔyԑkyerԑ fa aduane a ԑnni hɔ ne wɔn akatua a wɔate so no danee ɔyԑkyerԑ a na ԑtia ‘Communism’ no mu.
Ɛwom sԑ awieeԑ no Krushchev maa nkurɔfoɔ kɔsɔɔ ano deԑ nanso ɔmaa kwan maa nneԑma no bi yԑԑ adwuma sane tee aseԑ sԑ ɔde Wladyslaw Gomulka a na wagye din no bԑyԑ mansoafoɔ.
Na ‘Indus Valley Anibue’ no yԑ ‘Bronze Age anibue’ wɔ ‘northwest Indian’ mpɔtam hɔ a na seesei Pakistan ԑne mantam bi wɔ ‘northwest India’ ԑne ‘northeast Afghanistan’ ka ho.
Anibue no nyaa nkɔsoɔ wɔ ‘Indus River’ asase a ԑwɔ ne nkyԑn no so nti na edin no da so no.
Animdefo bi kyerԑ sԑ ԑnam sԑ na anibue no wɔ asase a ԑwɔ seesei asuo a awe ‘Sarasvati’ no nti ԑsԑ sԑ ne din yԑ ‘Indus-Sarasvati Anibue’, a ebinom nso frԑ no ‘Harappan Anibue’ ԑnam Harappa nti, beaeԑ a ԑdii kan wɔ 1920s no mu.
Sԑdeԑ na Roman empire no yԑ ‘militaristic’ si teԑ no na ԑmaa nnuroyԑ tuu mpɔn.
Emperor Augustus hyԑԑ aseԑ faa adɔkotafoɔ maa ɔyԑԑ ‘Roman Medical Corps’ a ԑdi kan no sԑdeԑ wɔde bԑyԑ adwuma ɔko akyi.
Na ‘Surgeons’ no wɔ nimdeԑ fa ‘sedatives’ ahodoɔ ho a ‘morphine ԑfiri poppy aba mu ԑne scopolamine a ԑfiri herbane aba mu’ ka ho.
Na wɔahunu sԑdeԑ wɔsi yi honam akwaa bi firi hɔ na amma deԑ wapira no annya ‘gangrene’ ԑne ‘tourniquets’ ԑnna ‘arterial clamps’ sԑdeԑ ԑbԑma mogya adi aforosane.
Mfeɛ ɔha a ɛtɔ so bebree akyi no, Roman empire no nyaa nimdeԑ pii wɔ nnuroyԑ ne apomuden mu a ԑno ne ԑnnԑ nimdeԑ no nnyinasoɔ.
‘Pureland origami’ yԑ ‘origami’ ԑma wotumi yԑ ‘fold’ baako pԑ wɔ berԑ bi mu, na wɔmma ‘folds’ a ne yԑ yԑ den te sԑ ‘reverse folds’ ho kwan ԑnna ‘folds’ no nyinaa wɔ baabi pɔtee a wɔwɔ.
John Smith na ɔyԑԑ no wɔ ‘1970s’ no mu de boaa wɔn a wɔnkwadaree ‘fold’ no yԑ mu anaa wɔnni ‘motor skills’ no pii.
Nkwadaa hunu abusua a wɔbɔ ԑne nneԑma a ԑwɔ abusua no ho ntԑm, saa nneԑma yi nso nya nsunsuansoɔ wɔ suban so.
Nhwԑsoɔ ne sԑ, nkwadaa a wɔhu wɔn abusua sԑ ԑsua na wɔnyԑ adeԑ wɔ sukuu mu no nso nyԑ adeԑ wɔ sukuu mu berԑ a wɔbԑhu sԑ saa adeԑ no bata n’abusua ho no.
Wɔ United States no, websaet a nkrɔfo kɔ hɔ paa a ɛto so mmiensa yɛ MySpaɔe. Na seiseiaa no, nkrɔfo a wɔn ho nsɛm wɔ hɔ no yɛ 54 million.
Nkrɔfo pii kɔ saa wɛbsaet ahorow yi hɔ, ne titirw adesuafo.
Saa websaet ahorow yi wɔ nneɛma pii a ɛyɛ wɔ ho. Ebi ne sɛ, ɛnyɛ den koraa sɛ wobɛbue klass kraatafa a nneɛma a ɛwɔ hɔ no bi ne blɔgs, sini ahorow, mfoni ahorow ne nkekaho ahorow.
Websaet address biako pɛ no bɛtumi de wo akɔ saa kraatafa no so. ɛyi ma no yɛ mmrɛw ma asukuufo a wɔbrɛ sɛ wɔbɛkae na watypo wɔ kiibɔd so anaa wɔɔspɛɛle no.
Wobetumi asesa no na ayɛ mmrɛw sɛ wobɛkenkan, na kɔla no nso wobɛtumi ayɛ no gɔɔn ana ketewaa bi.
Attention Deficit Disorder "yԑ adwene mu haw a deԑ ԑkyerԑ no ase ne ‘wobԑyԑ biribi a wonnwene ho’, ‘sԑ wode w’adwene bԑsi deԑ ԑnhia so, ԑne ‘sԑ wobԑpere wɔ biribi ho, anaa wobԑnya ahoɔden ama aboro so".
Ɛnyԑadesua dԑmdie na mmom ԑyԑ adesua haw; ԑyԑ "nkadwaa ɔha mu abupԑn 3 kɔsi 5, ebia ԑbԑyԑ Amerika nkwadaa ɔpepem mmienu".
Nkwadaa a wɔwɔ ADD ntumi mfa wɔn adwene nsi nneԑma bi te sԑ sukuu dwumadie so, nanso wɔbԑtumi de wɔn adwene akɔ biribi a wɔpԑ ne yԑ so te sԑ wɔrehwԑ cartoons a wɔn ani gye ho anaa wɔretwerԑ ɔkasamu a agyinahyԑdeԑ nni mu.
Saa nkwadaa yi taa nya asԑm ԑfiri sԑ "wɔda suban a ԑnyԑ adi, taa ne afoforɔ ko, sɔre tia mpaninnie" sԑdeԑ ԑbԑma wɔn adwene no ayԑ adwuma ԑfiri sԑ kwan a wɔn adwene no yԑ adwuma no yԑ soronko.
ADD toto ayɔnkofa a wɔne wɔn mfԑfoɔ wɔ ntam ԑfiri sԑ nkwadaa foforɔ ntumi nte deԑ nti a wɔda saa suban no adi anaa deԑ nti a ‘wɔbobɔ atwerԑdeԑ a ԑwɔ asԑmfua no sԑdeԑ wɔyԑ no no, anaa wɔn adwene mu mueeԑ.
Sԑdeԑ tumi a nnipa fa so nya nimdeԑ sane sua adeԑ no sesaeԑ sԑdeԑ yԑaka wɔ soro hɔ no, mprԑ dodoɔ a obi nya nimdeԑ no nso sesaeԑ.
Kwan a wɔfa so nya nimdeԑ bi no yԑ soronko. Na kwan a wɔfa so kaekae nneԑma no nyԑ ankorԑankorԑ deԑ bio na mmom sԑ wobԑkae abasԑm no na na wɔhwԑ.
Deԑ ԑteԑ ne sԑ, ‘Renaissance’ yԑԑ nsesaeԑ mapa wɔ kwan a yԑfa so sua adeԑ ԑne kwan a yԑfa so de nimdeԑ ma mu.
Na ‘akaatia’ no mfa wɔn nsa nnante bio anaa mfa nkuta adeԑ anaa mfa nto wɔn ho mfa nnua ntam te sԑ wɔn nsԑsoɔ asoroboa nkaeԑ no.
Akaatia nsa ne ne nan nyinaa kԑseԑ ne ne tenten yԑ pԑ, ԑkyerԑ nsa no dwumadie sԑ ɔnante ne nan so a.
Nnipa nsa yԑ tia sene ne nan, ԑmu nkasԑԑ no tene.
Nkasԑԑ a adi mfeԑ ɔpepem mmienu kɔsi ɔpepem mmiԑnsa no daa no adi maa yԑhunuu sԑ nsa dwumadie ne adeԑ mu sosɔ na mmom ԑnyԑ nanteԑ.
Ebinom gye di sԑ wobԑso daeԑ bebree wɔ berԑ a w’ani wɔ wo ho so na wonim sԑ woreso daeԑ no yԑ ahomete.
Deԑ nti a saa adeԑ yi ne ‘lucid dreams’ no a ԑretrԑ wɔ berԑ yi mu wɔ ‘REM states’ no mu no.
Sԑ wonya ‘REMs’ kakra bi anadwo baako biara a, saa berԑ a wobԑda pa ara ama wo nnipadua no agye n’ahome no ntaa nsi mma nyԑ ɔhaw.
Wei yԑ ahomete te sԑ deԑ ԑsԑ sԑ wosɔre simma aduonu anaa aduasa biara hwԑ TV no.
Ɛso nsunsuansoɔ no gyina sԑdeԑ w’adwene no bԑyԑ saa daeԑ yi bi anadwo biara.
Efiti mfiase no ara na nneɛma ankɔ yiye mma Italifo no wɔ North Afrika. Italifo hyɛɛ ɔsatu ase June 10,1940. Saa naawɔtwe no ara na na Britainfo asraafo kuo 11th Hussars ako agye Capuzzo Aban wɔ Libia afa.
Britainfo no kɔtɛw Bardia apueifam na wɔkyeree Italifo no asraafo mfiriyɛfo panyin a na ɔtɔ so du, Ɔsahene Lastuɔɔi.
Wɔ Ayɛwohomumɔ 28 so no, Marshal Italo Balbo, Libia Amrado-Sahene ne nea na ɛda adi pefee sɛ obedi adeɛ, Mussolini, wui bere a na wɔn wimhyɛn no resi wɔ Tobruk. Wɔn asraafo tuo na ekum wɔn.
Ɛnnɛyi agodie a wɔfrɛ no "fencing" no wɔ afa ahodoɔ bebree, efi adesuafoɔ a wɔwɔ sukuupɔn mu kosi wɔn a wɔreyɛ adwuma ne Olympic akansie mu.
Wɔtaa di saa agodie yi wɔ ntɔkwa kwan so, ɔgodifoɔ baako reko tia ne yɔnko.
Golf yɛ agodie bi a agodifoɔ no de mporibaa bɔ bɔɔlo no hyɛ tokuro mu.
Wɔde ntokuro dunwɔtwe na edi agurɔ yei mpɛn pii, na agodifoɔ no firi aseɛ wɔ tokuro a edi kan wɔ agodibeaeɛ hɔ na wowie wɔ deɛ ɛtɔ soɔ dunwɔtwe no so.
Ɔgodifoɔ a obewie agorɔ no berɛ a ɔto n'aporibaa no mpɛn kakraa bi no na odi nkonim.
Wodi saa agorɔ yei wɔ ɛserɛsoɔ, na wotwa ɛserɛ a etwa tokuro no ho ahyia no ma ɛyɛ tiatiaa sene deɛ aka no na wɔfrɛ no ahabammono.
Ɛbɛyɛ sɛ nsrahwɛ a agye din paa ne deɛ ɛfa akwantuo ho a nnipa anigye ho: Anigyediɛ nsrahwɛ.
Yei ne berɛ a nkurɔfoɔ kɔ mmeaeɛ a ɛda nso wɔ wɔn daa daa asetena mu de home na wɔde gye wɔn ani.
Mpoano, agodi beaeɛ ne beaeɛ a wosi ntomadan da mu yɛ beaeɛ a anigyediɛ nsrahwɛfoɔ tae kɔ.
Sɛ onii a ɔrekɔ beaeɛ bi no botaeɛ ne sɛ obesua beaeɛ no abakɔsɛm ne wɔn amammerɛ a, ende na wɔfrɛ saa nsrahwɛ yei sɛ amammerɛ nsrahwɛ.
Nsrahwɛfoɔ tumi kɔsra mmeaeɛ a agye din ahodoɔ wɔ kuro pɔtee bi mu anaasɛ wɔpaw sɛ wɔde wɔn adwene besi beaeɛ baako pɛ soɔ.
Berɛ a wohunuu deɛ ɛrekɔ soɔ no, atukɔtenafoɔ no ma wɔde asraafoɔ no bi bɛkaa wɔn ho.
Asraafoɔ a wɔbɛkaa wɔn a wodi anim no ho no ne 1st ne 3rd Hampshire asraafoɔ kuo a wɔyɛ mmarima 200, a na wɔhyɛ Colonel John Stark ne James Reed (a wɔbɛyɛɛ asahene) aseɛ.
Stark mmarima no gyinaa beaeɛ a atukɔtenafoɔ no wↄ wↄn atifi fam wↄ ɛban no ho.
Berɛ a asorɔkye no baa fam no, ɛmaa kwan bɛdaa Mystic asubɔtene no ho wɔ asase a na nsuo atwa ho ahyia ne fa bi atifiapueeɛ mantam hɔ. Ntɛm ara na wɔde aboɔ yɛɛ ban tiatia bi trɛɛ wɔn hyeɛ mu kosii mpoano ketewa bi wɔ nsuo no ano atifi fam.
Gridley ne Stark de dua a ne tenten bɛyɛ anammɔn 100 (30 m) sii ɛban no anim na ɔhyɛe sɛ obiara ntu tuo kosi sɛ wobewie deɛ ɛsɛ sɛ wɔyɛ.
Na Amerikafoɔ no tirimupɔ ne sɛ wɔbɛto ahyɛ wɔn so wɔ akwan ahodoɔ mmieɛnsa soɔ denam toto a wɔbɛtoto wɔn nneɛma yie.
Ɔsahene John Cadwalder bɛto ahyɛ Britainfoɔ asraafoɔ a wɔrebɔ ban wɔ Bordentown de atwe wɔn adwene firi hɔ, sɛdeɛ wobetumi asi mmoa biara a ɛbɛba ho kwan.
Ɔsahene James Ewing de asraafoɔ 700 betwa esubontene no wɔ Trenton Ferry, na wɔde wɔn nsa bɛto nsamsoɔ a ɛwɔ nsuka no so na woasi atamfoɔ no asraafoɔ no kwan na woantumi annwane.
Asraafoɔ dɔm a wobedi ako no ankasa betwa asubontene no akwansini nkron wɔ Trenton atifi fam, na wɔbɛkyɛ wɔn mu ekuo mmienu, kuo baako hyɛ Greene aseɛ na baako nso hyɛ Sullivan aseɛ, sɛdeɛ wɔbɛto ahyɛ wɔn so ansa na ahemadakye aduru.
Esiane sɛ wɔasesa mmirikatuo no firi anan mu nkyekyemu baako kɔ ɛfa no nti, ama ahohyɛsoɔ hu abehia sene ahoɔhare.
Ne saa nti ɛsɛ sɛ obi a wakwadare mmirika a wotu no akwansini fa no, tumi de sima mmienu so nkonim, ɛsɛ sɛ ne ho yɛ hare deɛ nanso ɛsɛ sɛ otumi hyɛ ne ho so wɔ akwansideɛ ahodoɔ a obehyia no mu.
Ansa na mmirikatuo berɛ no bɛhyɛ aseɛ no, nsiesie pa a wobetumi ayɛ ne sɛ wode wo ho bɛhyɛ mmirika a wotu fa kuro mu awɔbrɛ mu na wode apɔmutenetene a ɛyɛ ma nipadua ne fa ewɔ soro no ka ho.
Nnuane pa a yedie nkoa rentumi mma yɛnkɔ kan wɔ akansie mu, nanso ebetumi aboa akansifoɔ a wɔyɛ afoforɔ no apɔmuden.
Akwahosan a edi mu, nsuo a yɛtaa nom ne te a yɛbɛte sɛdeɛ nnuru a yɛde si nnuane anan mu no yɛ adwuma fa no bɛboa mmirikatufoɔ ma wɔakɔ wɔn anim na wɔn ani agye agodie no ho.
Amirikatuo a ɛnyɛ tenten pii yɛ akansie a ne boɔ nhyɛda nyɛ den; nanso, nkorɔfoɔ wɔ adwene bi wɔ nneɛma kakra a ehia na ama wɔatumi asi akan no.
Wobetumi atɔ ɛho akadeɛ sɛdeɛ wo berɛ a wohia, nanso ɛrenhyɛda nya nsunsuansoɔ biara wɔ deɛ wobɛyɛ no so.
Agodifoɔ no bɛte nka sɛ wohia akadeɛ bi ɛberɛ a saa ade korɔ no mfa mfasoɔ papa biara mmrɛ no.
Yebetumi aka sɛ atom yɛ nneɛma a eka bom yɛ matter no deɛ edi mu akotene paa.
Sɛdeɛ Bohr nhwɛsoɔ a wɔatwa no tia no kyerɛ no, ɛyɛ adeɛ a ɛyɛ nwonworann paa, a electron no redi nucleus no a ɛwɔ ne mfinfini no ho kyinhyia te sɛ sɛdeɛ okyinsoroma twa owia no ho hyia no. Hwɛ mfonini 1.1.
Nneɛma nketenkete mmienu ɛna ɛbom yɛ nucleus no - neutrons ne protons.
Proton no wɔ anyinam tumi a ɛyɛ positive na neutron no nni tumi biara. Electron no wɔ anyinam tumi a ɛyɛ negative.
Ansa na wobɛhwɛ opirafo no, ɛsɛ sɛ wodi kan hwɛ beaeɛ a ɔda no yie na woamfa wo ho anto asiane mu.
Bere a worebɛn no no, ɛsɛ sɛ wohwɛ beaeɛ a opirafo no da ne biribiara a ebetumi ayɛ asiane nso.
Sɛ wo a worekɔboa opirafo no nso pira a, eyi bɛma tebea no asɛe koraa.
Nhwehwɛmu ama ada edi sɛ berɛ a obi abotow, ehu aka no na ɔma adeɛ yɛ hu sene sɛdeɛ ɛteɛ no na ɛde ɛyeaa ne mmerɛwyɛ ba wɔn a wɔn akyi ase yɛ wɔn ya no mu.
Nsunsuansoɔ a wɔn a wɔma adeɛ yɛ hu sene sɛdeɛ ɛteɛ no nya no na ɛma wɔhyehyɛɛ nnawɔtwe biara PA nhyiamu no na ɛnyɛ abotow ne ehu ntira.
Sɛ yɛreka adwene pa a wonni wɔ ɛyeaa ho a ɛne sɛ wobehu nsonsonoe a eda ɛyeaa koankorɔ ne honam yeaa esaine ahokeka no a, wɔn a wɔyɛ adwuma berɛ nyinaa no‪ behia mmoa yie.
Hunu a yehunu adeɛ no gyina yɛn akwaa a ɛma yehunu adeɛ no anaa aniwa no so.
Nneɛma ahodoɔ a ɛda nsow na wɔde ayɛ aniwa no, na emu ntiaseɛ yɛtumi yɛ nworanworan denam nkwaboa no ahiadeɛ so.
Sɛdeɛ wɔyɛɛ emu biara ɛnna ahoɔden soronko ɛwɔ, ehu han ahodoɔ ntɛm na ne namyɛ nso nyɛ pɛ. Afei nso, ɛsono deɛ ebehunu biara ne sɛdeɛ ɛbɛte aseɛ na sɛ ɛbɛyɛ adwuma yie a, ehia nɔma ahodoɔ.
Population yɛ abɔdeɛ no dodoɔ a wɔn nnyinaa te asaase ne fa pɔtee bi so.
Sɛ akorankoro nnyinaa a wɔte asaase no beae pɔtee bi no di nsɛ paa wɔ nipadua no su ahodoɔ a ani tumi hu ho a, wɔfrɛ wɔn abɔdeɛ a wɔn suban yɛ baako.
Sɛ akorankoro biara da su pɔtee bi adi akwan ahodoɔ ahodoɔ so a, wɔfrɛ wɔn abɔde a wɔn suban gu ahodoɔ.
Ntatea bom sɛ ekuo nante na wɔhome wɔ akwan ahorow pii so.
Sɛ a wɔretwa kwan no, ntatea yi nante anwumerɛ na wɔhome bereɛ a ade akye.
Kuo no fi ase twa kwan berɛ a aduane a ɛwɔ hɔ no so ateɛ. Eduru saa berɛ yi a, da biara kuo no yɛ esie ahodoɔ na ɛnkyɛ na wɔasesa no.
Saa akwantwa anaa nanteɛ yi di bɛyɛ nna 17 berɛ biara.
Dɛn ne nkwammoaa? Asɛmfua nkwammoaa firi Latin asɛmfua "cella", a deɛ ɛkyerɛ ne "ɔdan ketewa bi", na wodii kan de saa asɛmfua yi dii dwuma berɛ a na obi a ɔhwɛ nneɛma nketenkete a aniwa ntumi nhnuu mu no rehwɛ sɛdeɛ wɔahyehyɛ nsatire no mu no.
Nkwammoaa no ne ade titiriw a abɔdeɛ a nkwa wɔ mu nkwa nyinaa gyina so, na abɔdeɛ nyinaa wɔ nkwammoaa yi baako anaa deɛ ɛboro saa.
Nkwammoa ho hia paa titire berɛ a yeresua nkwa ho adeɛ no, kyerɛ sɛ, wɔtaa frɛ wɔn "ntayaa a wɔde hyehyɛɛ nkwa".
Amemene no hwɛ ma biribiara kɔ so pɛpɛɛpɛ wɔ nipadua no mu. Na ɛyɛ saa berɛ a ɛde anyinam nketenkete fa ntini no mu na ama mogya adi aforosiane a biribiara nsi ne kwan wɔ nipadua no mu.
Anyinam nketenkete a ɛfa ntini no mu no tumi kɔ ntɛm paa wɔ nipadua no mu na eyi bɔ nipadua no ho ban fi ɛyea biara a ɛbɛsɔre ho.
Sɛ wode atɔyerɛnkyɛm ahodoɔ toto ho a, mframa gyampantrudu si wɔ beaeɛ ketewa bi nanso ɛsɛe biribiara a ɛda ne kwan mu no.
Mframa gyampantrudu tutu nnua a esisi hɔ, ɛwae nnua a ɛbobɔ dan so, na ɛma kaa so to kɔ wiem. Mframa gyampantrudu a ano yɛ den paa no mu ɔha mu nkyem mmienu pɛ tumi di boro nnɔnhwere mmiɛnsa.
Wɔ ahum akɛse paa mu no, mframa no anoɔden no tumi duru 480 km/h (133m/s; 300 mph).
Nnipa akɔso ayɛ ahwehwɛniwa na aboa ma wɔahu nneɛma nketenkete mfeɛ mpempem pii nie.
Nanso, wodii kan yɛɛ ahwehwɛniwa a wɔde hwɛ wiem ankasa wɔ Europa wɔ afeha a ɛtɔ so 16 no awieiɛ no mu hɔ.
Wɔde ahwehwɛniwa ahodoɔ mmienu na ɛbom yɛ saa ahwehwɛniwa a wɔde hwɛ wiem no na etumi ama nneɛma a ɛwowɔ akyire no abɛn na ayɛ akɛseɛ nso.
Adwuma a yɛyɛ no bɛnkorɔ no kyerɛ sɛ, sɛ nnipa dodoɔ no ara nya so mfasoɔ a wobetumi anya pii berɛ tiawa mu sɛ wɔyɛ pɛsɛmenkomenya a. Ɛno nti adufudepɛ ne pɛsɛmenkomenya ne yɛn bɛtena daa.
Yɛhwɛ kwan sɛ, nnipa dodoɔ no ara behunu sɛ deɛ ɛbɛboa ne sɛ wɔne afoforɔ bɛbom ayɛ adwuma.
Nnipa pii daeɛ so ne sɛ wobetumi atukwan akɔhwɛ nsoroma foforɔ ne wiase foforɔ, ebinom dwennwen dea ɛwɔ hɔ ho ebinom gye di sɛ amanfrafoɔ anaa adeɛ foforɔ a nkwa wɔ mu na ɛwɔ okyinsoroma foforɔ bi so.
Nanso, sɛ wei bɛsi mpo a ɛbɛkyɛ paa ansa na esi. Nsoroma no ntɛm atete ma akwansin ɔpepemhuhaa na ɛda nsoroma a wɔye "efipamfoɔ" ntam.
Ebia dakorɔ, wo nanankansewanom begyina amanfrafoɔ wiase bi so na wɔbɛ dwennwene wɔn nananom ho?
Nkwanmoa pii na ɛwɔ mmoa mu. Wɔdi biribiara na ɛyam no wɔ nipadua no mu. Mmoa pii tumi keka wɔn ho.
Mmoa nkoaa na wɔ wɔ adwene (nanso ɛnyɛ wɔn nyinaa na wɔ wɔ bi; jellyfish, sɛ nhwesoɔ no, enni adwene).
Yehu mmoa wɔ wiase yi mu baabiara. Wotutu fam, wodware wɔ ɛpo mu, na wotu wɔ ewiemu.
Nkwanmoa yɛ abɔdeɛ (nnoɔma) a nkwa wɔmu fa ketewa bi.
Nkwammoa (cells) fi Latin asɛmfua cella mu a ɛkyerɛ ɔdan ketewa.
Sɛ wohwɛ nkwammoa wɔ microscope aseɛ a, wobehu sɛ ahinanan anaa kukuruwa na ayɛ no ma.
Abɔdeɛ a nkwa wɔmu ho adesuani, Robert Hooke a ofi England, de microscope huu ahinanan nketewa a ɛwɔ cork mu.
Wɔte sɛ adan. Ɔno ne nipa a odi kan a ohuu nkwanmoa a wɔn awuwu.
Nnoɔma ne nnoɔma afrafra betumi asesa efiri tebea baako mu akɔ foforɔ mu a ɛnsesa.
Nitrogen yɛ ogyamframa a ɛsan tesɛ nitrogen a ɛsen. Ne nsesen mu no emu yɛ duru nanso emu nnoɔma no yɛpɛ.
Nsuo nso yɛ nhwɛsoɔ foforɔ. Hydrogen atoms ne oxygen atoms na ɛwɔ nsuo mu.
Ɛwɔ saa nhyehyɛ no pɛpɛɛpɛ sɛ ɛyɛ ogyamframa, dea ɛsen, anaa nea ɛyɛ den.
Ɛmfa ho sɛ sɛdeɛ ɛte betumi asesa no, n'aduru mu deɛ ɛnsesa.
Mmerɛ yɛ adeɛ a ɛwɔ yɛnkyɛn aberɛ biara, na ɛka deaɛ yɛyɛ biara, nanso yɛntumi nte aseɛ.
Nyamesomfoɔ, nyansapɛfoɔ ne nyansahufoɔ de mfe boro ɔpepem na asua mmerɛ ho adeɛ.
Yehu sɛ mmerɛ yɛ nnoɔma a esisi mmɔho abakɔsɛm a efi nnɛ berɛ mu de kosi tete berɛ mu.
Mmerɛ nso yɛ sɛdeɛ yɛ de nnoɔma a esisi bɛtoto sɛdeɛ ɛkyɛ (tenten) ho.
Wo ankasa wobetumi asusu sɛdeɛ mmerɛ kɔ sɛ wohwɛ sɛdeɛ nnoɔma pɔtee sisi a. Nnoɔma pɔtee a esisi ntuatua so yɛ nnoɔma a ɛkɔ so sisi bere ne bere mu.
Kɔmputa a ɛwɔ hɔ nnɛ no wɔde yɛ sini nketewa ne mfoni ho adwuma.
Sinitwa a aba soɔ no wɔde kɔmputa na ɛyɛ, na saa sinitwa a ɛte saa nu woyi no paa wɔ TV so ne sini ahodoɔ mu.
Wɔtae de kɔmputa ahodoɔ a aba so no na etwa nnwom na wɔkeka ngyigyeɛ ahodoɔ bɔmu.
Efiti bere tenten wɔ mfe ɔpepem akrɔn ne mfe ɔpepem aduonu bere mu no, na wɔgyedi sɛ nnipa a wɔdii kan tenaa New Zealand yɛ Maorifoɔ, a na nnoma akɛseɛ a wɔferɛ wɔn moas na wɔkyere wɔn sɛ wɔkɔ ahayɔ a.
Nsɛm no san kyerɛɛ sɛ Maorifoɔ no to fii Polynesia wɔ Great Fleet na wɔ bɛgyee New Zealand fii Moriorifoɔ no nsam, na wɔbɛtee akuafoɔ asafo.
Nanso no, adanseɛ foforɔ kyerɛ sɛ na Moriorifoɔ no yɛ Maori asaase no fa kɛseɛ mu foɔ a wɔfi New Zealand kɔɔ Chathan Nsuopoɔ so, na wɔfii aseɛ yɛɛ wɔn nnoɔma foforɔ, amammerɛ a asomdwo wɔmu.
Na abusuakuo foforɔ bi nso wɔ Chathan nsuopɔ no so wei yɛ Maorifoɔ a wɔtu fii New Zealand.
Wɔferɛɛ wɔn ho Moriorifoɔ na abenne die kakra wɔ hɔ na ewi aseɛ no, wɔpopaa Moriorifoɔ no fi hɔ.
Ankorɛankorɛ a na wɔka ho bɛyɛ mfenhyia du bi no boaa yɛn ma yɛn ani sɔɔ nea yetumi yɛ ne dea yɛn ani gye ho aberɛ a yɛsusu yɛn akwansideɛ ne mpo nkuguodie ho no.
Aberɛ a yɛɛtie ankorɛankorɛ sɛ wɔka wɔn ho, wɔn abusua, ne wɔn adwumayɛbea ho nsɛm no, yɛbɛnyaa nhumu a edi mu fa tete ho ne nnipa bi a wɔnyaa kuo no ho nneɛma pa ne nneɛma bɔne ho nkɛntɛnsoɔ.
Aberɛ a wore te obi abakɔsɛm aseɛ no nkyerɛ sɛ wote n'amammerɛ aseɛ, nanso no ɛboa ma wonya baabi a wɔgyina wɔ kuo no mo abakɔsɛm ho adwene.
Aberɛ a wɔ susu wɔn nkunimdie na wɔhu wɔn nkuguodie ho no, ankorɛankorɛ ne kuo no mu foɔ a wɔgusu sua adeɛ no nyinaa behu kuo no so mfasoɔ, kuo no botaeɛ ne deɛ ɛma kuo no kɔ so.
Wɔ saa tebeaɛ wei mu no, kae a wɔ kae adwuma ho suban a esisi atwam ne nkunimdie a ɛde baeɛ no boaa nkuroɔfoɔ ma wɔ buee nsesaeɛ foforɔ ne nkyerɛkyerɛ foforɔ maa kuro no mu asɔre no.
Saa nkunimdie ho asɛm wei maa nsakraeɛ ho hu no kɔɔ fam, aberɛ nso a na ɛreda daakye ho nsakraeɛ adi wɔ wɔn mu.
Adwenkoro nhwɛsode ye ɔhaw anosɔ kwan a ɛka nsusuii ahorow anaa nimdeɛ ahorow bom de sɔ ɔhaw ano.
Saa adwenpɔ yi botae ye amirika, enidiso, nokwasɛm, bio nso nokwasɛm a wɔbɛhyɛ no nsow, akwan ahorow a wɔbɛsan de adi dwuma bio, ne nsɛm a wɔbɛboaboa ano.
Adeɛ a ɛho hia paa fa saa adwenpɔ yi ho ne sɛ: mmuae baako pɛ na ɛwɔ hɔ. Wodwen mmuae mmienu pɛ ho, a ɛne woatwa anaa woaten.
Saa kwan a wɔfa so dwen no hyɛ nyansahu anaa gyinapɛn bi ase.
Nkrɔfo a wɔwɔ saa adwene no dwen nnidisonnidiso, no wɔtumi kyere ade a ɛyɛ sɔnnahɔ gu wɔn tirim, sɔw ɔhaw ano, na wɔtumi yɛ nyansahu mu nhwehwɛmu ho adwuma.
Nnipa na ɛyɛ mmoa a wɔwɔ adom akyɛdeɛ a wɔ de hu deɛ afoforɔ dwene.
Wei kyerɛ sɛ yetumi de yɛn adwene bu deɛ afoforɔ susu ho, deɛ wɔn abɔ wɔ tirimu sɛ wɔbɛyɛ, deɛ wɔgyedi, deɛ wɔnim anaa deɛ wɔpɛ.
Deɛ ɛka saa nnoɔma a yɛetumi yi ho no, afoforɔ nsusuyɛ a yɛbɛte aseɛ no ho hia paa. Ɛma yɛn kwan ma yɛtumi di nnoɔma a ɛsisi ma yɛhu a ɛho nteaseɛ yɛ akɛseɛ ho dwuma.
Sɛ nhwɛsoɔ no, sɛ ɛba sɛ wuhu sɛ obi repae hyɛn bi mfɛnsere a, wobetumi asusu sɛ ɔrebɔ mmɔden awia obi a ɔnnim no hyɛn.
Wobɛbu no atɛn wɔ ɔkwan foforɔ so sɛ wayera ne hyɛn no nsafoa na ɛyɛ ɔnoa ne hyɛn na ɔrebɔ mɔden sɛ ɔbɛbu awura mu a.
MRI gyina abɔdeɛ ho nimdeɛ a wɔferɛ no nuclear magnetic resonance (NMR) gyinapɛn so, na Felix Bloch (ɔyɛ adwuma wɔ Stanford University) ne Edward Purcell (ofi Harvard University) na wɔ huu ho adeɛ wɔ 1930s mu.
Wɔ saa resonance wei mu no, baabi a tweboɔ wɔ ne akasafidie ho mframa ma atoms de akasafidie ho adafitwa sɛnkyerɛne nketenkete ma.
Wɔ afe 1970 mu no, Raymond Damadian, a ɔyɛ oduruyɛfoɔ ne nhwehwɛmu ho nyansapɛfoɔ, huu nea enti a wɔde tweboɔ ho dede ho mfonini yɛ adwinnade a wɔde yɛ nyarewa mu nhwehwɛmu.
Mfe anan akyi no wɔde ɛho tumi maeɛ, ɛno na na ɛyɛ wiase nyinaa tumi a edi kan a wɔde maeɛ wɔ MRI adwumayɛ ho.
Wɔ 1977 mu no, Dr, Damadian wie “whole-body” MRI nhwehwɛmu afidie a edi kan no ho adwumayɛ, na ɔferɛɛ no ”Indomitable”.
Nkɔmmɔbɔ a ɛnkɔ so wɔ berɛ baako mu no boa yi berɛ ma adwennwene ne sɛdeɛ yɛne afoforɔ di.
Ɛma kwan ma asuafoɔ tumi yɛ adwuma wɔ wɔn ankasa berɛ mu na wɔn ankasa di berɛ a wɔde yɛ ɔkasa ho nkyerɛkyerɛ.
Deɛ ɛka ho no, anohweteɛ kakra wɔ mmerɛ a yebetumi de ayɛ adwuma no so. (Bremer, 1998)
Wiase ntontan kɛseɛ a yɛde yɛ adwuma no ma adesuafoɔ kwan ma wɔnsa tumi ka nsɛm aberɛ biara.
Adesuafoɔ nso betumi de wɔn nsɛmmisa ama akyerɛkyerɛfoɔ aberɛ biara wɔ da no mu na wɔbetumi ahwɛ kwan sɛ wɔbenya muaeɛ ntɛm, sen sɛ wɔbɛtwɛn akosi da foforɔ a wɔde behyia bio.
Ɔkwan a wɔfa so sua adeɛ a ɛbaeɛ wɔ ɛnnɛ berɛ yi mu akyi no ma yɛde yɛn ho fi deɛ obiara gye di sɛ ɛyɛ ho. Yenni ɔkwan pa baako a yɛfa so sua adeɛ.
Nokorɛ ne sɛ, yenni ade baako a ɛsɛ sɛ yɛ sua. Adesua kɔ so wɔ osuahunu a ɛkɔ so wɔ osuani ne nimdeɛ a ɛda n'anim.
Osuahunu a yɛwɔ wɔ wankasa-yɛ ne nsɛm a yɛde ma, TV so dwumadie a agyina adesua so kyerɛ sa gyinapɛn wei.
Yɛn mu pii hwɛ TV so dwumedie a ɛma yɛhu sɛdeɛ nnoɔma kɔ so anaa yɛnya osuahunu a yɛremfa yɛn ho nhyɛ mu anaa yɛremfa saa nimdeɛ no nyɛ adwuma.
Yɛrentumi ɛnsiesie hyɛn, ensi nsuti wɔ yɛn dan akiyi, yɛrentu kwan ɛnkɔ Peru nkɔ hwɛ tete nnoɔma a asɛi, anaa yɛbɛ siesie yɛn fiepamfoɔ dan.
Nnaase nkɔ ma nsuo aseɛ fiber optic cable links a ɛkɔ Europe ne broadband satellite no, Greenland man no wɔ so bi na emu nnipa bɛyɛ 93% na wɔwɔ wisae ntotan kɛseɛ no so.
Wo ahɔhoɔdan (sɛ wɔ te ahɔhoɔdan nketewa mu anaa wɔn ankasa wɔn fie mu) mu no wɔ betumi anya wifi anaa kɔmputa a ɛwɔ wiase ntontan kɛseɛ no so, na ɛhɔ foɔ nyinaa wɔ wiase ntontan kɛseɛ adan anaa mmeaeɛ bi a wɔwɔ amansan wifi.
Sɛdeɛ yeadi kan ahu no, ɛmfa ho sɛ w’agye asɛmfua "Eskimo" atom wↄ United States no, wↄ Canada no, arcticfoↄ a wↄnnyɛ United Statesfoↄ hu no sɛ ɛyɛ atɛmdidie.
Ɛmfa ho sɛ wobɛte sɛ "Greenland" ↄmanfoↄ no de asɛmfua no redi dwuma no, ɛsɛ sɛ ahↄhoↄ kwati sɛ wↄbɛbↄ.
Wↄn a wofi Greenland no frɛ wↄn ho Inuit ne kalaalleg (duduoↄ kabea: Kalaallit) wↄ Canada, na wↄn man mu deɛ, wↄfrɛ wↄn Greenlandfoↄ.
Wɔ Greenland no, wonnim sɛ sɛdeɛ wobedi ahɔhoɔ bɔne anaa wɔbɛdwene ne ho adwene bɔne. Wɔ kuro no mu mpo, "beaeɛ a ɛhɔ nyɛ" nni hɔ.
Awɔ ne tebea a ɛnyɛ a onii a ɔmmoaboaa ne ho no behyia.
Sɛ wokɔ Greenland awɔw mmerɛ a (berɛ a worekɔ atifi fam no, na awɔw no mu reyɛ den), ɛho hia sɛ wode ntadeɛ ɛka hye ba.
Kyɛ a wobɛkyɛ wɔ ɔhyew mmere mu no betumi ama wo nna ho aba asɛm na woanya apɔmuden mu haw so.
Sɛ ɔhyew mmerɛ ba a, hwɛ wo ho yie wɔ Nordic ntontom ho. Ɛmfa ho sɛ wɔmma yareɛ biara no, wotumi ha adwen paa.
Berɛ a wɔkyerɛ sɛ San Francisco sikasɛm gyina nsrahwɛ mmeaeɛ a ɛkyɛn so a ɛwɔ hɔ no so no, onya sika firi mmeaeɛ ahodoɔ pii.
Ne fa a ɛde adwuma ba paa ne wɔn a wɔyɛ ɔfese, aban, sikasɛm, adwadie na nsrahwɛ nnwuma no.
Da a wɔtaa da no adi wɔ wɔn nnwom, sini, nwoma, ɛne amammerɛ a agye din mu no ama kuro no ne nneɛma a ɛyɛ fɛ wo mu no ama ne din ahyeta wɔ wiase afanan nyinaa.
San Francisco asisi nsrahwɛ mmeaeɛ akɛseɛ a ahɔhogyebea ahodoɔ, adidibea, ɛne nhyiamu asa a ɛho twa.
San Francisco yɛ mmeaeɛ a ɛyɛ sene biara wɔ ɔman no mu baako a wobenya a Asiafoɔ nnuane: Koreafoɔ, Thailandfoɔ, Indiafoɔ, ne Japanfoɔ.
Ɔkwan a wotu kɔ Walt Disney World yɛ akwantuo a ɛho hia pa ara wɔ Amerikafoɔ mmusua beberee mu.
Nsrahwɛ a "yɛhwɛ kwan" ne sɛ yɛde wiemhyɛn bɛkɔ Orlando Wiemhyɛn gyinabea, yɛbɛtena bɔɔso mu akɔ Disney ahɔhogyebea a ɛwɔ hɔ ara, yebedi bɛyɛ nnawɔtwe wɔ Disney asase so, na yɛasan aba fie.
Nkyerɛkyerɛ mu no gu ahodoɔ, nanso yei ne deɛ nnipa dodoɔ no ara kyerɛ berɛ a wɔka sɛ "wɔrekɔ Disney World no".
Tekiti beberee a wɔtɔn wɔ intanɛt so denam badwam adetɔn wɛbsaet bi te sɛ eBay anaa Craigslist so no yɛ tekiti a wɔde edi dwuma kakra a wo nso wobetumi de edi dwuma boro da baako akɔ mmeaeɛ ahodoɔ.
Berɛ a yei yɛ biribi a ɛkɔ so wɔ hɔ paa no, Disney bra saa adeyɔ yi: wɔmfa tekiti a obi de edi dwuma nsan mma obi foforɔ.
Sɛ wobɛpɛ sɛ woda ntomadan mu wↄ' Grand Canyon ɛhyeɛ no akyi a, ɛho behia sɛ wonya tumi krataa a wↄde kↄ nkuro nketewa a ɛwↄ akyiri no bi.
Tumi krataa a wↄde ma no sua sɛdeɛ ɛbɛbↄ canyon no ho ban, na wo nsa beka tumi krataa yi bosome da edi kan, abosome anan a ansaana saa bosome no ahyɛase.
Ne saa nti, ↄpɛpↄn da a edi kan na wobenya tumi krataa a wↄde kↄ nkuro nketewaa ansa na woatumi akↄ hↄ kotonimma bosome mu.
Beaeɛ a wosi ntomadan da mu a agye din bi te sɛ "Bright Angel Campground "a ɛwↄ "Phantom Ranch" nkyenmu no taa yɛ mã ntɛm da a edi kan a wↄma hokwan sɛ nsrahwɛfoↄ betumi abegye ato hↄ no.
Tumi krataa a ɛwↄ hↄ ma wↄn a wↄba hↄ begye yɛ kakraa bi; nea odi kan ba na ɛnya.
Sɛ wode kaa bewura Southern Africa yɛ ɔkwan pa a wode behunu sɛdeɛ mantam no fɛ teɛ ne mmeaeɛ ahodoɔ a enni nsrahwɛ kwan ankasa no so.
Sɛ woyɛ wo nhyehyeɛ yiye a, wobetumi de kaa biara ayɛ saa nanso wotu fo sɛ wode 4x4 bedi dwuma na mmeaeɛ bi deɛ 4x4 a n'ase wɔ soro nkoaa na wobetumi de akɔ hɔ.
Hyɛ no nso berɛ a woreyɛ nhyehyeɛ no sɛ ɛmfa ho sɛ Southern Africa wɔ asomdwoe no, ɛnyɛ aman a etwa ne ho ahyia no nyinaa na ɛte saa.
Visa ho ahwehwɛdeɛ ne ɛho ka da nso wɔ ɔman biara mu, na ɔman a wofiri muo no nso nya ɛso nkɛntɛnsoɔ.
Ɔman biara nso wɔ mmara soronko a ɛkyerɛ mpofirim nneɛma a wohia wɔ wo kaa mu.
Victoria Falls yɛ kuro a ɛda Zimbabwe atɔeɛ fam, ɛwɔ Livingstone, Zambia hyeɛ no agya na ɛbɛn Botswana.
Kuro no da nsuo a ebu fa soɔ no nkyɛn pɛɛ, na ɛno ne beaeɛ a ɛyɛ fɛ titire a ɛtwetwe nkurɔfoɔ, na saa nsrahwɛbea a agye din yi ma wɔn a wɔn ani gye anigyedeɛ a esaine wɔ mu ho ne bɛhwɛadefoɔ hokwan ma wɔtena hɔ kyɛ.
Wɔ osutɔberɛ (Obubuo kosi Ɔbɛnem) mu no, nsuo no dodoɔ kɔ soro na nsuo a ebu fa soɔ gye ntrɛha.
Ɛyɛ deɛ wo ho bɛfɔ ɔkwan biara so sɛ wobetwa nsamsoɔ no anaasɛ wobɛfa anammɔn kwan a akyiakyia a ɛbɛn nsuo a ebu so no.
Wɔ ɔkwan foforɔ soɔ no, esaine nsuo no dodoɔ a ɛkɔ soro paa nti ɛbɛyɛ den sɛ wobehunu nsuo a ɛrebu fa soɔ no yie—nsuo no bebrebe ntira!
Tutankhamun Nna (KV62). KV62 betumi ayɛ nna a agye din sene biara wɔ subɔn no mu, sɛdeɛ wɔ 1922 Howard Carter hwehwɛ hunuu ɔhene kumaa no ahenfo afunsieɛ a na ɛte sɛ deɛ wɔmfaa nsa nkaaɛ no.
Sɛ yɛde toto ahenfo a aka no nna no mu dodɔ no ho dea, ɛho nhyɛda nhia sɛ wɔbɛkɔ Tutankhamun nna hɔ nsrahwɛ, esaine sɛ esua koraa na deɛ wɔde asiesie mu no nnɔɔso nti.
Obi biara a ɔbɛpɛ sɛ ohunu sɛdeɛ afunu a wɔakora so no asɛe akoduru berɛ a wɔbɔɔ mmɔden sɛ wobeyi afiri afunu adaka no mu no abam bebu efiri sɛ ne ti ne n'abatire nkoa ara na obehunu.
Sika a na wɔde ahyehyɛ nna no nni hɔ bio, na wɔde ne nyinaa kɔ Egyptfoɔ Akoradebea a ɛwɔ Cairo.
Ɛbɛyɛ papa sɛ nsrahwɛfoɔ a wonni mmerɛ no bɛkɔ mmeaeɛ afoforɔ akɔhwɛ hɔ.
Phnom Krom da Siem Reap anaafoɔ atɔeɛ fam 12 km. Wosii saa asɔredan a ɛwɔ koko no so wɔ afeha a ɛtɔ so 9 mu, berɛ a na Ɔhene Yasovarman di adeɛ no.
Beaeɛ a asɔredan no wɔ no kusuuyɛ ɛne sɛdeɛ wohu no hɔ berɛ a wohwɛ hɔ firi Tonle Sap ɔtadeɛ no ma kokoɔ no foro yɛ deɛ mfasoɔ wɔ so.
Sɛ wokɔsra beaeɛ hɔ a, wobetumi de kodoɔ nso atu kwan akɔ beaeɛ a ɔtadeɛ no wɔ.
Wohia Angkor Pass na woatumi awura asɔredan no mu. Eno nti ɛnsɛ sɛ wo werɛ firi sɛ wobɛfa wo paspɔt berɛ a worekɔ Tonle Sap.
Yerusalem yɛ Israel kuropɔn ne kuro a ɛso paa, ɛmfa ho sɛ aman afoforɔ ne Amanaman Nkabom no nnye ntom sɛ ɛhɔ yɛ Israel kuropɔn.
Tete kuro a ɛwɔ Yudafoɔ nkokoɔ no mu no abakɔsɛm a ɛyɛ anika no edi mfeɛ mpempem pii.
Kurow no yɛ kronkron ma ɔsom ahodoɔ mmieɛnsa a wɔgye di sɛ Onyankopɔn yɛ baako - Yudasom, Kristosom, ne Kramosom. Na ɛha abɛyɛ honhom, ɔsom, ne amammerɛ beaeɛ ama wɔn.
Esaine hia a kuro no ho hia wɔ ɔsom adeyɔ mu ne ne titire no mmeaeɛ a ɛwɔ Old City mpɔtam hɔ no nti, Yerusalem yɛ beaeɛ a nsrahwɛfoɔ kɔ paa wɔ Israel.
Yerusalem wɔ abakɔsɛm, fam tutu ne amammerɛ mmeaeɛ, na wɔsan wɔ sotɔɔ akɛseɛ, annoneɛtɔnbea, ne adidibea a nkorɔfoɔ ayɛ mu ma na ahokeka ne anigyeɛ wo mu wɔ hɔ.
Ecuador hwehwɛ sɛ Cuba manfoɔ no nya nsatoɔ krataa ansa na woafa amanaman wiemhyɛnbea anaa ɛhyeɛ ahodoɔ so ewura Ecuador.
Ɛsɛ sɛ Ecuador Suafoɔ a ɔhwɛ Amannɔne Nsɛm so no de ne nsa hyɛ saa krataa yi ase.
Woayɛ saa ahwehwɛdeɛ yi na ama akwantuo ho nhyehyeɛ a ɛda aman mmienu yi ntam no ayɛ deɛ nhyehyeɛ da ho.
Ɛsɛ sɛ Cuba manfoɔ a wokura US krataa a ɛma wɔn kwan ma wɔtena hɔ no kɔ Ecuadorfoɔ nanmusini no asoeɛ hɔ na woyi no firi saa ahwehwɛdeɛ yi mu.
Ɛsɛ sɛ wo paspɔt no da ne kwan mu na abosome nsia san gu mmerɛ a ɛsɛ sɛ wotena hɔ no akyi. Wohia tekiti a ɛde wo kɔ san ba anaa tekiti a edi mmerɛ dodoɔ a ɛsɛ sɛ wotena hɔ no ho adanseɛ.
Nnipakuo nsrahwɛ boɔ yɛ fo, eno nti sɛ ɛyɛ wo nkoaa anaa wo ne adamfo bi no, bɔ mmɔden hyia afoforɔ na monhyehyɛ ekuo a nnipa bɛyɛ anan kosi nsia wo mu na ama ɔbaakofoɔ boɔ ayɛ deɛ ɛwɔ fam.
Nanso, ɛnsɛ sɛ yei ha wo, esaine sɛ mpɛn pii no wɔka nsrahwɛfoɔ no hyɛ kaa mu dodoɔ mu.
Ɛte sɛ deɛ wɔde daadaa nkurɔfoɔ ma ɛyɛ wɔn sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ wotua sika pii.
Bepɔ a emu dɔ na ɛware bi wɔ Machu Picchu atifi fam awiei hɔ, mpɛn pii no wobehunu sɛ ɛwɔ amanfo no mfonini akyi.
Ɛte sɛ deɛ ɛyɛ den berɛ a wogyina aseɛ no, na emu dɔ na ɛyɛ den sɛ wobɛforo akɔ soro, nanso nnipa a wɔwɔ ahoɔden betumi de sima 45 aforo akɔ soro.
Wɔde aboɔ no ayɛ anammɔnkwan no atrapoe no mu dodoɔ no ara, na wɔ beaeɛ a emu dɔ no wɔde dadeɛ ayɛ adeɛ woso mu de foro kɔ soro.
Wɔ deɛ yɛaka yi mu no, hwɛ kwan sɛ wobɛhome hyeehyee, na hwɛ wo ho yie wɔ mmeaeɛ a emu dɔ, ne titire no berɛ a woafɔ, esaine sɛ ebetumi ayɛ hu nti.
Ɔbodan ketewa bi bɛn soro hɔ a ɛsɛ sɛ wofa mu, emu sua kakra na ɛsɛ sɛ wo mia wo ho fa mu.
Sɛ worekɔhwɛ mmeaeɛ ahodoɔ ne mmoa ne mfudeɛ wɔ Galapogos a, ɛbɛyɛ papa sɛ wode kodoɔ, sɛdeɛ Charles Darwin yɛe wɔ 1835 mu no.
Po so ahyɛn bɛboro 60 na ɛfa Galapagos nsuo no so - a wotumi fa nnipa dodoɔ firi 8 kosi 100.
Nnipa dodoɔ no ara di kan kora beaeɛ a wɔbenya no so (esaine sɛ kodoɔ no taa yɛ ma paa wɔ).
Hwɛ hunu sɛ onii a wobɛfa ne so akora no yɛ Galapagos nimdefoɔ a ɔwɔ ahyɛn ahodoɔ ho nimdeɛ.
Yei bɛma woagyina deɛ w'ani gye ho ne deɛ wompɛ so apaw ɛhyɛn a ɛne no behyia.
Ansa na Spainfoɔ no reba wɔ afeha a ɛtɔ so 16 mu no, na Inca di Chile atifi fam no so berɛ a kuromma a wɔfrɛ wɔn Araucanians (Mapuche) no te Chile mfimfini ne anaafoɔ fam.
Mapuchefoɔ no yɛ tete Amerikafoɔ kuo a wɔade wɔn ho no mu baako a woanfa wɔn ho anhyɛ wɔn a wɔka Spainfoɔ kasa no tumidie ase kosi berɛ a Chile nyaa fawohodie.
Ɛmfa ho sɛ Chile nyaa fawohodie wɔ 1810 (berɛ a Napoleon ko no maa Spain bɛdaa hɔ a na onni aban a edi so bɛyɛ mfeɛ bi no), wɔantumi anye wɔn ho amfiri Spainfoɔ no nsam kosi 1818.
Dominican Republic (Spainfoↄ kasa: Republica Dominicana) yɛ Caribeanfo kurow a ɛda hispaniola apuei mantam, na ɛne Haiti na ɛbↄ hyeɛ.
Sɛ yɛde ne mpoano a anwea fitaa aye so ma ne mmepↄw a atwa ho ahyia no to nkyɛn a, ehↄ na wubehu Europe kuro keseɛ a akye yie wↄ Americas hↄ, a afei eka Santo Domingo ho.
Tainofoↄ ne Caribefoↄ na wodii kan bɛtenaa supo no so. Na Caribefoↄ ka Arawakan kasa no, na wↄbaa hↄ wↄ afe 10,000 ansaana yɛn berɛ yi mu.
Wↄ Europe nhwehwɛmufoↄ no mmaeɛ, mfeɛ kakra bi akyiri no, Spainfoↄ a wobedii Tainosfoↄ no so no maa wↄn dodoↄ no so tee koraa.
Sɛdeɛ Fray Bartolome de las Casas (Tratado de las Indias) kyerɛ no, efiri afe 1492 kosi 1498 mu no, Spainfoↄ a wobedii wↄn soↄ no kumkum Tainofo bɛyɛ 100,000.
Jardin de la Union. Wɔyɛɛ saa beaeɛ yi sɛ asa maa ahotefoɔ fie no wɔ afeha a ɛtɔ so 17, nanso Templo de San Diego pɛ ne dan a aka si hɔ.
Seesei wɔde ɛhɔ ayɛ adwadibea kɛseɛ, na dwumadie kɔ so wɔ hɔ ɛberɛ biara, anɔpa ne anadwo.
Adidibea ahodoɔ etwa turo no ho ahyia, wɔyɛ kɔnsɛte a wongye hwee awiaberɛ ne anwummerɛ biara firi central gazebo.
Callejon del Beso (Mfeano kwan). Abranaa mmienu a kwan a ɛda ntam yɛ sɛntimita 69 yɛ tete ɔdɔ ho anansesɛm fie.
Sɛ woma mmofra bi sika ketewa bi a, wɔbɛka anansesɛm yi akyerɛ wo.
Bowen Island yɛ da akwantuo anaa nnawɔtwe awieɛ nsrahwɛ a wɔma kayak so akwantuo, hiking, aguadie beaɛ, adidie beaeɛ ne mmeaɛ ahodoɔ pii.
Mpɔtam a edi mu yi wɔ Howe Sound wɔ Vancouver nkyɛn, na wotumi kɔ hɔ a wommerɛ denam nsuo so hyɛn ho nhyehyɛe efiri Granville Nsuopɔ so wɔ downtown Vancouver.
Wɔn a wɔn anigye abɔntennim agorɔdie ho no, Sea to Sky corridor ho nanteɛ no hia wɔn paa.
Whistler (dɔnhwerew 1.5 hyɛnka afi Vancouver) asetena boɔ yɛ den nanso agye din paa esane 2010 Winter Olympics no enti.
Wɔ awɔbereɛ mu no, fa wo ho hyɛ nsuokyerɛma so agorɔdie a ɛyɛ paa no bi mu wɔ North America, na ahohuruberɛ mu no sɔ bepɔ so sakre twe a ɛyɛ papapaa no bi nso hwɛ.
Ɛsɛ sɛ wogye hokwan to hɔ ansa. Ɛsɛ sɛ wonya hokwan no ansa na wobetumi atena Sirena ama adeɛ akye.
Sirena nkoaa na ɛyɛ kwaeɛhwɛfoɔ atenaeɛ a ɛma kwan ma nnipa mmienu anaa deɛ ɛboro saa da na wɔma aduane a ɛyɛ hye na abɔnten nsraban mu da ka ho. La Leona, San Pedrillo, ne Los Patos ma abɔnten nsraban mu da a aduane nnka ho.
Wobetumi agye turo ho kwan tee afi Kwaeɛhwɛfoɔ Atenaeɛ wɔ Puerto Jiménez, nanso wɔngye credit cards
Turo Adwumayɛbea (MINAE) no mma turo hokwan nto hɔ ma no nntra bosome baako a wɔsusu sɛ obi de bɛba no.
CafeNet El Sol ma kwan ma wo kora beaeɛ no so to hɔ na wɔgye US$30, anaa $10 ma wo twa da-koro; ɛho nsɛm wɔ Corcovado kratafa no so.
Cook nsuopɔ no yɛ nsuopɔ ɔman a ɛne New Zealand bɔ fekuo, ɛwɔ Polynesia, wɔ Anaafoɔfam Pacific Ɛpo no mfinimfini.
Ɛyɛ nsuopɔ kuo a ɛwɔ nsuopɔ 15 a apete ɛpo 2.2 million km2 so.
Esane sɛ wɔne Hawaii wɔ berɛ baako mu nti, wɔ tae ferɛ nsuopɔ no "Hawaii down under".
Ɛmfa ho sɛ esua no, ɛkae ahɔhoɔ a wɔn mfe akɔ anim no sɛdeɛ na Hawaii teɛ ansa na ɛdee ne ho ne ahɔhoɔdan akɛseɛ ne mpuntuo ahodoɔ.
Kuropɔn biara nni Cook nsuopɔ no so na ɛmom nsuopɔ 15 na ɛwɔ so. Deɛ ɛyɛ emu titire yɛ Rarotonga ne Aitutaki.
Wɔ aman a atu mpɔn nnɛ so, a wɔma ɛmpa a ɛyɛ papa ne anɔpaduane nso no wɔn ama no anya nkɔanim ama abɛyɛ soronko.
Wɔ soro hɔ pɛɛ no, B&Bs si akan wɔ neama titire mmienu ho: ɛmpa ne anɔpaduane.
Sɛdeɛ ɛteɛ no, ɛwɔ mmeaeɛ a ɛtete saa no ɛsɛ sɛ obi si gyinaeɛ sɛ obenya ɛmpa a ne boɔ yɛ den, ebia mpasotam a wɔde nsa ayɛ anaa tete ɛmpa a ne boɔ yɛ den.
Nnuane a ɛba berɛ ne berɛ mu wɔ ɔmantam no mu no wɔtumi de yɛ anɔpaduane anaa aduane a ɔhɔhoɔ no pɛ.
Beaɛ no betumi ayɛ tete ɔdan a agye din a wɔde tete neama asiesie mu, saare a wɔn atwa no kama ne beaɛ a wɔdware nsuo.
Sɛ wobɛtu w'ankasa wo hyɛn de atu kwan tenten wɔ lɔre kwanso no yɛ adeɛ a ɛho hia obiara esani sɛdeɛ ɛnyɛ kyɛnkyerɛkyɛnn no nti.
Ɛnte sɛ hyɛn akɛseɛ no, wo nim sɛdeɛ woka wo hyɛn no deda na wonim hyɛn no ahoɔden.
Sɛ wosi ntomadan wɔ w'asase so anaa wɔ kuro mu a ɛmfa ho sɛdeɛ ne kɛseɛ te no ɛnyɛ den sɛ ɛbɛ twetwe nkurɔfoɔ adwene aba wo so.
Ne tia twa mu no, w'ankasa wo hyɛn a wode bɛ fa lɔre kwan so atu kwan a ɛnyɛ adeɛ a nkurɔfoɔ tae yɛ no yɛ ɔkwan a wɔfa so "camp".
Hyɛn mu akwantuo betumi ayɛ yie sɛ wo wɔ minivan kɛseɛ, SUV, Sedan anaa Station Wagon a wotumi bu nkɔnnua no mu ma no da hɔ a.
Ahɔhoɔ dan no bi wɔ abakɔsɛm a afi sika kɔkɔɔ bere mu wɔ keteke kwan so ahuruhuro ne ɛpo so hyɛn akɛseɛ berɛ so; ansana Wiase Nyinaa Ko a ɛtɔ so mmienu no, wɔ 19th anaa 20th centuries mfitiaseɛ no.
Na saa ahɔhoɔ dan wei yɛ beaɛ a na asikafoɔ a wɔn agye din no tena, na wodi nnuane pa na wɔde wɔn ho hyɛ anigyediɛ a ɛkɔ so anadwo mu.
Wɔn tete fittings a atwam, neama a aba soɔ a wɔnni bi, ne wɔn tetesɛm a anuonyam wɔ mu no nyinaa ka wɔn suban no ho.
Ɛwɔ mu sɛ ɛnyɛ ɔman adeɛ deɛ, nanso ɛtɔ da bi a wɔgye ahɔhoɔ bi tesɛ aman mpanyinfoɔ na atitire ahodoɔ.
Ɔkwantofoɔ a ɔwɔ sika paa no betumi asusu ho sɛ obetu kwan akɔ wiase nyinaa, na watena tena saa ahɔhoɔ dan ahodoɔ pii wei mu.
Ahɔhoyɛ adwumayɛbeaɛ kuo yɛ bi kuo a wɔ ka akwantufoɔ ne ɔmanfoɔ a wɔwɔ nkuro a wɔ kɔ so no bɔ mu.
Sɛ wopɛ sɛ wɔ de wo ho ka kuo wei ho a deɛ ahia ne sɛ wo bɛ hyehyɛ krataa bi wɔ wiase nyina ntontan so; nanso ebia wɔde nhyehyɛeɛ foforɔ bɛ ma wo anaa wɔ bɛ hia neama bi aka ho ansa na adi mu.
Afei wɔbɛma wo ahɔhoɔ dan ahodoɔ a ɛwɔ hɔ no nyinaa din wɔ krataa so anaa wɔ wiase nyinaa ntontan so, ɛtɔ da bi a wɔbɛma wo ntotoho ne mpɛnsɛnpɛnsɛnmu a ahɔhoɔ afoforɔ ayɛ nso.
Wɔ firi couchsurfing aseɛ wɔ Ɔpɛpɔn 2004 mu aberɛ a kɔmputa so dwumedieyɛfoɔ Casey Fenton nyaa ewiemuhyɛn mu akwantuo a ne boɔ wɔ fam de kɔɔ Iceland akyire no nanso na onni baabi a ɔbɛ tena no.
Ɔde email maa asuafoɔ a wɔwɔ ɔman no suapɔn no mu na onyaa wɔn mu beberee a wɔpenee so sɛ ɔmɛ tena wɔn nkyɛn a wɔrengye no hwe.
Wɔn a wɔ hwɛ ahɔhoɔ dan so no tae yɛ mmranteɛ ne mmbabaawa – a wɔn adi bɛyɛ mfe aduonu – nanso wobetumi ahu ahɔhoɔ a wɔyɛ mpanyinfoɔ nso wɔ hɔ.
Worentae nhu abusua a mɔfra ka ho wɔ hɔ, nanso ahɔhoɔ dan bi ma wɔn hokwan wɔ adan a ɛyɛ kokoamu dan mu.
Beijing kuro a ɛwɔ China no na ɛyɛ kuro a Olympic Winter Games wɔ 2022 no bɛkɔ so wɔ mu, na ɛno bɛma no ayɛ kuro a adi kan a ahohuruberɛ ne awɔberɛ mu Olympics bɛkɔ so wɔ mu.
Mfitiaseɛ ne awieɛ dwumadie no bɛkɔ so wɔ Beijing na dan mu nsuokyene dwumedie no nso bɛ kɔ so wɔ hɔ.
Nsuokyɛrɛma so agudie ahodoɔ bɛ kɔ so wɔ Taizicheng nsuokyɛrɛma agudiebeaɛ hɔ wɔ Zhangjiakou, bɛyɛ 220 km (140 miles) fi Beijing.
Asɔredan no pii yɛ afahyɛ afe biara afi Obubuo awieɛ kosi Kotonima mfinimfini, na ne sesa a ɛsesa no gyina asɔredan biara ne n'afe biara abunna nhoma so.
Wɔdi asɔredan no afakyɛ pii ka asɔredan no afidie ho anaa onyame a ɔhwɛ asɔredan no awoɔda anaa dwumedie titire biara a ɛfa asɔredan no ho no.
Kerala asɔredan afahyɛ yɛ anika paa, ne asono a wɔn asiesie wɔn fɛfɛɛfɛ a wɔ sa wɔn santene, asɔredan adwontofoɔ ne afahyɛ afoforɔ.
World's Fair (a wɔtae ferɛ no World Exposition, anaa ne teawa mu no Expo) yɛ amanaman ntam adwinni ne abɔdeɛ mu nyansapɛ ho afahyɛ.

International Horticultural Expositions yɛ dwumadie soronko a ɛda nhwiren, afifideɛ turo ne biribiara a ɛfa nnua ho adi.
Ɛwɔ mu sɛ wɔ nsɛmka mu no wɔbetumi ayɛ no afe biara (aberɛ a wɔwɔ aman afoforɔ so), nanso wɔntae nnyɛ.
Saa dwumadie ahodoɔ wei tae kɔso wɔ abosome mmiɛnsa ne nsia ntam, na wɔyɛ wɔ asase bɛyɛ 50 hectares so.
Wɔwɔ sini yie ho akwan pii a wɔde adi dwuma mfe a atwa mu yi. Standard 35 mm film (36 by 24 mm negative) yɛ deɛ obiara nim.
Sɛ ɛsa pɛ wobetumi ahyɛ no ma biom sɛ ɛsa a, na ɛho mfonini bɛyɛ tesɛ DSLR a aba so no.
Medium-format sini ho mfonintwa mfidie de 6 by 6 cm yɛbea na ɛyɛ adwuma, te sɛ 56 by 56 mm negative pɛpɛɛpɛ.
Wie ma nsakraeɛ bɛyɛ mpɛn anan te sɛ nea ɛyɛ 35 mm negative (3136 mm2 versus 864).
Mmoa a wɔn ho yɛ hu ka mfonini ho adwuma a ɛyɛ den paa ma mfoninitwafoɔ, na ɛhia nsiadeɛ papa, aboterɛ, suahunu ne adwinnadeɛ ɛyɛ papa a wɔn aka abɔ mu.
Mpɛn pii no wɔnkyerɛ mmoa a wɔn ho yɛ hu ho mfonini twa ho anisɔ, nanso tesɛ mfoninitwa biara no, mfonini biara som bo tesɛ nsɛmfua apem.
Mmoa a wɔn ho yɛ hu ho mfonini twa ɛtaa hia telephoto ahwehwɛ, ɛmfa ho sɛ nneama bi tesɛ nnomaa kuo anaasɛ abɔdeɛ nketewa bi hia ahwehwɛ afoforɔ.
Mmoa a wɔfiri aman foforɔ so pii ho yɛ nna, na ɛtɔ da a turo no wɔ mmra a ɛfa mfonin a wotwa ma aguadi botae no ho.
Mmoa a wɔn ani so yɛ den betumi afɛre adeɛ anaa wɔn ayɛ keka. Mpɔtam hɔ betumi ayɛ nwunu, hyehyeehye, anaasɛ ɛdɔm.
Wiase no wɔ kasa ahodoɔ bɛboro 5,000, a akasafoɔ bɛboro aduonu ne ɔpepem 50 ka ho.
Mpɛn pii no ɛyɛ mmerɛ sɛ wobɛte nsɛm a wɔtwerɛ aseɛ sen nsɛm a wɔka, nso. Wei yɛ nokorɛ titire wɔ akwankyerɛ ho, a ɛtaa yɛ den sɛ wobɛbɔ din no wɔ nteaseɛ mu.
Amanfoɔ no nyinaa dodoɔ naa ka Borɔfo kasa yie, nea ɛsen saa no wobetumi ahwɛ nimdeɛ a ɛwɔ ɔhye kwan - ne titire wɔ nnipa a wɔsusua mu.
Fa no sɛ, sɛ wo bɛyɛ a, Manchester ni, Bostwana ni, Jamaica ni ne Sydney ni a wɔte adiediepon ho redi anwummerɛ aduane wɔ adiediebea bi mu wɔ Toronto.
Wɔ de anansesɛm a efiri wɔn kuro mu gyegye wɔn ani, wɔka wɔ wɔn kasa a ɛda nsow mu ne wɔn kokoam kasa titire mu.
Aduane a wɔtɔ wɔ aguadibea a abaso no taa yɛ ɔkwan a ɛyɛ fo a wobɛtumi anya aduane adi. Sɛ aduane yɛ akwannya ɛnni hɔ a, aduane a wɔasiesie deda na wɔpaw.
Aguadiebea a abaso no nya nduane a wɔn asiesie no deda ahodoɔ pii ho nkɔsoɔ. Ebinom nso ma afidie a wɔde ka aduane hye anaa wɔ fa akwan foforɔ so ka aduane hye.
Wɔ aman bi so anaasɛ adekoradan ahodoɔ mu no anyɛ yie koraa no adidibea baako wɔ hɔ, mpɛn pii no nea nhyehyɛe ɛnni ho a wɔn boɔ wɔ fam.
Yɛ na fa wo amansɛm ho nsɛsoɔ ne nipa a ɔyɛ nsiakyibaa no ɔfrɛ ho nsɛm ka wo ho.
Ehia sɛ wɔde nipa ko a ɔyɛ nsiakyibaa no e-mail akwankyerɛ ne amanaman ahomatorofoɔ akontahyɛdeɛ kyerɛ na wɔma wo ɛho afuotuo/tumi ne ade pere.
Nya ne sɛso foforɔ wɔ wo bɔtɔ mu ne wiase nyinaa ntontan so (mane wo ho fa e-mail so fa akadeɛ no ka ho, anaa kora so wɔ "cloud").
Sɛ wode laptop anaa tablet retu kwan a, kora ne sɛso no bi wɔ ne nkaeɛ anaasɛ ne nkaeɛ afidie so (wonhia wiase ntontan keseɛ ansa na wonsa aka).
Afei nso fa ɔmansem/ɔfrɛ sɛso ma akwantuo mu ayɔnkofoɔ ne abusuafoɔ anaasɛ nnamfoɔ a wɔwɔ fie na wɔwɔ ɔpɛ sɛ wɔbɛboa no.
Torɔn (ɔsan nso de Ɔforɔteɛ kɔkɔɔ) ɛnyɛ keka firi awoɔ mu, nanso wɔbɛbɔ wɔn ho ban sɛ wɔte nka sɛ biribi bɔ wɔn hu a.
Sɛ nnipa nnhu sɛ torɔn ho betumi ayɛ hu a, ebia wɔ bɛ bɛn no dodo na wɔ de wɔn ho bɛ to amaneɛ mu.
Sԑ worenom nsa a susu. Nsa ho nsunsuasoɔ gyina onipa ko no so nti sԑ wohunu deԑ wohia a, ԑho hia pa ara.
Nsanom mmorosoɔ ho nsunsuasoɔ a wobԑtumi anya no daakye ne bi ne sԑ wo brԑboɔ bԑsԑe, w’ani bԑfira anaa wobԑwu. Sԑ wonom nsa a ne yԑ no tia mmara a, ԑma saa ɔhaw no yԑ kԑse.
Nsa a ne yԑ tia mmara no bԑtumi awɔ nneԑma a ԑnyԑ bi te sԑ, ‘methanol’ wom a ԑbԑtumi ama anifira anaa owuo asi wɔ berԑ a wobԑfa ketewa bi mpo.
Ahwehwԑniwa boɔ bԑtumi ayԑ fo wɔ amannɔne aman so, ne titire ne aman a sikasԑm ne akatua wɔ fam.
Hwԑ sԑ wobԑsɔ w’ani ahwԑ wɔ fie, ne titire ne sԑ nsiakyibaa bi wɔ hɔ na fa ԑho akwankyerԑ no ka wo ho na wɔde ayԑ biribi wɔ baabi foforɔ.
Ahwehwԑniwa a agye din a ԑwɔ saa mmeaeԑ no bԑtumi anya haw mmienu; ԑbi nyԑ papa, ԑnna deԑ ԑyԑ papa a wɔakra no boɔ yԑ den sene deԑ wɔayԑ wɔ ɔman no mu no.
‘Kɔfe’ yԑ adeԑ baako a wɔdi ho dwa wɔ wiase yi mu na wotumi ahunu n’ahodoɔ wɔ wo mpɔtam hɔ.
Nanso, akwan ahodoɔ soronko bi wɔ hɔ a wɔfa so nom kɔfe wɔ wiase afanan nyinaa a ԑho hia sԑ wohunu.
‘Canyoning (anaa: canyoneering) yԑ sԑ wobԑkɔ ‘canyon’ ase, a ԑbԑtumi aba sԑ awo anaa nsuo wom.
‘Canyoning’ ka yeinom bom, nsudware, adeforo, ԑne huri--nanso ԑhia atenetene kakra bi anaa wo tebea na woatumi ahyԑ aseԑ (sԑ wode toto mmepɔ foforɔ, ‘scuba’ twi anaa ‘alpine skiing’, sei ho a).
‘Hiking’ yԑ dwuma a wɔdi wɔ abɔntene a ԑyԑ nanteԑ wɔ atenaeԑ a ԑnyԑ nnipa na ayԑ, mpԑn pii wɔ ‘hiking trails’ so.
Ɛda ‘Hiking’ yԑ beaeԑ a ԑnsua nsene kwansini baako kɔsi kwan tenten a wobԑtumi de da baako atwa.
Sԑ ԑyԑ da ‘hike’ a wobԑyԑ no kwan a ԑnyԑ den so a, ahoboa kakra bi na wohia, ԑnna obi a ne ho yԑ den kakra bi bԑtumi atwi.
Abusua a wɔwɔ mma a wɔsusua no bԑhia ahoboa bebree, nanso da koro abɔntene pue no, mmɔfra nketewa ne wɔn a wɔahyԑ sukuu ase no bԑtumi.
Wiase mu no, ‘tour’ adwumakuo a wɔyԑ adwuma bԑyԑ sԑ 200 na ԑwɔ hɔ. Dodoɔ no ara na wɔn a wɔyԑ wɔn adwuma.
‘Global Running Tours’ nsiananmu no, ‘Go Running Tours’ wɔ nkorabata bebree wɔ beaeԑ a aman bebree wɔ ahodoɔ nan mu.
Wɔn ase firi ‘Barcelona Running Tours Barcelona ԑne Copenhagen Running Copenhagen’ akyԑre na ‘Running Tours Prague’ a ԑwɔ Prague ԑne afoforɔ bԑkaa wɔn ho.
Nneԑma bebree wɔ hɔ a ԑsԑ sԑ wohwԑ ansa na woatu kwan akɔ baabi.
Sԑ wotu kwan a, nhwԑ anim sԑ wobԑnya no te sԑ deԑ "ԑwɔ fie no". Obuo, mmara, aduane, ‘trafike’, baabi a wobԑda, deԑ ԑyԑ, kasa, ne deԑ ԑkeka ho bԑsesa afiri deԑ ԑwɔ baabi a wofiri no ho.
Wei yԑ adeԑ bi a ԑsԑ sԑ ԑhyԑ w’adwene mu, sԑdeԑ ԑbԑyԑ a w’abam mmu anaa wo bo mfu sԑdeԑ wɔyԑ nneԑma wɔ hɔ.
Wɔn a wɔboa akwantufoɔ awɔ hɔ firi ‘19th century’. Wɔn a wɔboa akwantufoɔ no yԑ sԑ ԑboro ɔkwantuni no suahunu ma abɔdeԑ, amammerԑ, kasa anaa aman a adwumayԑfoɔ sika wɔ fam a so.
Ɛwom sԑ wɔn a wɔboa akwantufoɔ bebree wɔ ɔpԑpa sԑ wɔbԑgye kwan a ԑwɔ fam, nanso bebree hwԑ akwantuo soronko bi so, sikasԑm a ԑwom anaa baabi a worekɔ.
Ɛyԑ sԑ wobԑfa obi a ɔtaa di akwantuo a ԑte sԑ wo deԑ no ho dwuma.
Hwԑ akwantuo a ɔrebɔ ho dawuro no, wɔ wԑbsate so anaa wɔ ‘shop window’ so.
Sԑ wopԑ sԑ wohunu wiase no wɔ berԑ a wommrԑ ho, sԑ ԑhia nti, sԑdeԑ woyԑ nneԑma, anaa akan bi a, akwan bi wɔ hɔ a wofa so yԑ saa.
Saa nneԑma no gu ahodoɔ mmienu: Sԑ wobԑyԑ adwuma wɔ berԑ a woatu kwan anaa hwԑ sԑ wobԑte wo ka no so. Saa atwerԑ yi fa deԑ ԑtwa toɔ no ho.
Wɔn a wɔbԑtumi atwa ahotɔ mu, ԑberԑ, ԑne deԑ ԑba daa sԑdeԑ wɔbԑte ka no so no, hwԑ ka a anyԑ hwee no wobԑbɔ wɔ akwantuo no mu.
Afotuo no ne sԑ, akwantufoɔ nwia adeԑ, nkɔ obi agyapadeԑ so, mfa wɔn ho nhyԑ dwadie a ԑnyԑ mu, nsrԑ adeԑ, anaa mmu nkurɔfoɔ mfa so.
Baabi a wɔhwԑ akwantufoɔ no yԑ baabi a ԑdi kan a wobԑhunu wɔ berԑ a woresi afiri wiemhyԑn, suhyԑn, anaa kaa foforɔ mu no.
Ketekye a ԑtumi wura ɔman foforɔ mu no, ԑmu no ara na wɔhwehwԑ nnipa no nti ԑsԑ sԑ wowɔ ID bi a ԑdi mu wɔ wo ho ansa na woaforo saa ketekye no mu baako.
Ketekye a wɔda mu no, deԑ ɔte ho no bԑgye ‘w’akwantuo krataa’ no sԑdeԑ ԑbԑyԑ a wɔnsԑe wo nna.
Sԑ wobԑtwerԑ wo din no ka visa no gyeԑ ho. Aman binom so no, ԑsԑ sԑ wokyerԑ mpɔtam hɔ mpanimfoɔ no sԑ woaba hɔ na woma wɔn baabi a woteԑ no addrԑsse.
Wei ho bԑhia sԑ wohyehyԑ ‘fɔm’ bi wɔ apolisifoɔ a wɔwɔ hɔ no hɔ anaa wɔn a wɔhwԑ akwantufoɔ nsԑm so no ɔfese hɔ.
Aman bebree a wɔwɔ saa mmara no, ahɔhogyebea no na wɔbԑhwԑ saa nhyehyԑeԑ no so (hwԑ sԑ wobԑbisa).
Deԑ ԑwom koraa ne sԑ, wɔn a wɔnte baabi a akwansrafoɔ teԑ no na wɔbԑ twerԑ wɔn din. Nanso, ԑmma wɔnhunu mmara no so nti pԑ ansa na woaduru.
‘Architecture’ hwԑ kwan a wɔfa so yԑ ‘nhyehyԑeԑ’ sane si adan so. Sԑdeԑ wɔasi asi dan bi no koraa tumi yԑ baabi a akwasrafoɔ tumi bԑhwԑ.
Adan bebree yԑ fԑ na sԑ wohwԑ firi dan tenten bi so anaa mpoma bi a ԑwɔ baabi yie a, ԑyԑ fԑ pa ara.
‘Architecture’ adwumayԑ no ne ebinom te sԑ ‘urban planning’, ‘civil engineering’, ‘decorative arts’, ‘interior design’ ԑne ‘landscape design’deԑ no na ԑkɔ.
Sԑ wohwԑ sԑdeԑ ‘pueblos’ nkuraa no bebree teԑ a, wontumi nnya anigyeԑ biara wɔ hɔ gye sԑ wotu kwan kɔ Albuquerque anaa Santa Fe.
Nanso, ‘casinos’ dodoɔ no ara a wɔabobɔ wɔ soro hɔ no ma anodeԑ, ԑnna wɔn mu bebree de anigyeԑ mu wɔn a wɔagye din ba (ahyԑaseԑ no na ԑyԑ wɔn a wɔatwa Albuquerque ԑne Santa Fe ho ahyia).
Yԑ ahwԑyie: baabi nketewa a wɔtɔ nsa wɔ ha no nyԑ mma ɔhɔhoɔ sԑ ɔbԑkɔ hɔ.
Adeԑ baako nso ne sԑ, New Mexico atifi fam no, wɔ haw pa ara wɔ adorɔbafoɔ a wɔnom nsa ka kaa ho, ԑnna adorɔbafoɔ a wɔaboro no taa wɔ baabi a wɔtɔ nsa nketewa no.
Mfonin anaa adeԑ a wɔayԑ ato ban ho a wɔmpԑ na yԑfrԑ no ‘graffiti’.
Ɛwom sԑ ԑbae akyԑ deԑ, nnipa bebree fa no sԑ mmabunu de ‘spray paint’ resԑe ɔman no anaa ankorԑankorԑ agyapadeԑ.
Nanso, seesei deԑ yԑwɔ ‘graffiti artists’, ‘graffiti events’ a wɔayԑ ԑne "mmara" ban. ‘Graffiti paintings’ wɔ saa nteaseԑ yi mu no sԑ ‘artworks’ sene ‘tags’ a wɔnhunu.
‘Boomerang’ toɔ yԑ nimdeԑ baako a akwansrafoɔ bebree pԑ sԑ wɔnya.
Sԑ wopԑ sԑ wosua sԑdeԑ wɔto ‘boomerang’ a ԑsane ba wo nsam a, hwԑ sԑ wowɔ ‘boomerang’ a ԑyԑ ma ne ba.
‘Boomerangs’ a ԑwɔ Australia no bebree nyԑ deԑ ԑsane ba. Ɛyԑ sԑ wɔn a wɔrehyԑ aseԑ no nto no ‘windy’
Wɔnoa ‘Hangi’ Aduane wɔ tokuro a ԑyԑ hye wɔ asase no mu.
Wɔde aboɔ a wɔayi afiri gyam na ԑma tokuro no mu yԑ hye anaa baabi wɔ hɔ a ‘geothermal heat’ ma baabi yԑ hye.
Wɔtaa de ‘hangi’ no noa anwummerԑ aduane a wɔtoto.
Mmeaeԑ bebree wɔ Rotorua ma ‘geothermal hangi’, wɔ berԑ a ‘hangi’ afoforɔ wɔ Christchurch, Wellington ԑne baabi foforɔ.
‘MetroRail’ wɔ nkyekyԑmu mmienu wɔ ketekye a ԑwɔ anaa ԑbԑne Cape Town: ‘MetroPlus’ (a wɔsane frԑ no First Class) ԑne Metro (wɔfrԑ no Third Class).
‘MetroPlus’ yԑ baabi a ahotɔ wɔ ԑnna nnipa no nnɔso wɔ hɔ nanso ne boɔ yԑ den kakra, nanso ԑyԑ fo sene metro tikiti a ԑwɔ Europe.
Ketekye biara wɔ MetroPlus ԑne Metro beaeԑ nyinaa bi; MetroPlus beaeԑ no taa wɔ ketekye no ano no a ԑbԑne Cape Town no.
Sԑ wokuta ma afoforɔ - Mma w’ani mfiri wo baage so da ne titire ne sԑ morewura ɔman foforɔ mu.
Wɔbԑma wo afa nnubɔne akuta wɔ berԑ a w’ani nna wo ho so na ԑba saa a, ɔbԑkɔ ɔhaw kԑseԑ pa ara mu.
Wei yԑ baabi a modidi soɔ, wɔbԑtumi de nkraman a wɔte nnubɔne mpampan aba berԑ biara a wɔmmɔ nkaeԑ.
Aman bi wɔ asotwe kԑse ma saa adeԑ yi pa ara mpo sԑ ԑyԑ berԑ a ԑdi kan a; wei bԑtumi ayԑ sԑ wobԑkɔ afiase mfeԑ 10 anaa wɔbԑku wo.
Baage a obiara nkɔ ho no, obi bԑtumi awia ԑnna ԑbԑma mpanimfoɔ ani aba ho ԑfiri sԑ wɔbԑsusu sԑ ԑyԑ topaeԑ.
Ɛnam sԑ da biara wo ne saa mmoawa yi di ahyia nti, biribiara kyerԑ sԑ wobԑtumi adi ahyia a wɔnnya nsunsuansoɔ biara.
Nanso wiase baabi foforɔ no, baabi a ‘bacteriological fauna’ no yԑ foforɔ ma wo no, wobԑtumi anya ɔhaw.
Bio nso, baabi a ԑhɔ yԑ hye no, ‘bacteria mmoawa’ no tumi nyini ntԑntԑm sane tena ase kyԑre wɔ berԑ a ԑnni nnipadua no mu.
Ɛno nti ne ɔhaw a ԑtoo Delhi Belly, Pharaoh's Curse, Montezuma's Revenge, ԑne wɔn nnamfonom no.
Sԑdeԑ ahome mu haw nyԑ nna wɔ baabi a ԑhɔ yԑ nwunu no, saa ara nso na nsono mu haw nyԑ nna wɔ baabi a ԑyԑ hye ԑnna mpԑn bebree ԑyԑ abofu nanso ԑnyԑ hu pa ara.
Sԑ woretu kwan wɔ ɔman a ɔretu mpɔn mu berԑ a ԑdi kan a, – anaa wiase yi mu baabi foforɔ a, – mԑnnwene sԑ wonhu biribi a ԑda nso firi w’amammerԑ ho.
Akwantufoɔ a wɔdi mu bebree ahyia biribi foforɔ wɔ wiase baabi a ԑretu mpɔn no ma adi wɔn so, baabi a woresesa wo ho afa amammerԑ bi ntԑm hia.
Ne titire ne wo nna a ԑdi kan no, hwԑ sԑ wobԑsԑe sika wɔ ‘Western-kwan’ ne ahɔhogyebea papa, aduane, ԑne biribi foforɔ a wohia ho na ԑmma wo ne hɔ mfa.
Mԑnna ‘mattress’ anaa ‘pad’ so wɔ fam wɔ beaeԑ a wonnim hɔ mmoa no.
Sԑ wobԑda abɔntene a, fa ‘camp cot’ anaa ‘hammock’ ka wo ho sԑdeԑ ԑbԑbɔ wo ho ban afiri awɔwɔ, nyanyankyerԑ ne wɔn a wɔtete saa no ho.
Ma kɔfe a ԑyԑ dԑ nwɔ wo fie hɔ anɔpa na ma ‘chamomile tea’ a yԑde dwodwo yԑn ho nwɔ hɔ anwummerԑ.
Sԑ woregye w’ahome wɔ baabi a ԑbԑne wo fie a, wowɔ mmerԑ a wode bԑyԑ wo ho yie na woagye w’ani.
Sԑ wopԑ sԑ wohunu nneԑma bi ano so a, fa saa akwanya yi na yam biribi a ԑyԑ dԑ:
ebia a wobԑhunu biribi anodeԑ bi a wobԑtumi ayԑ adi no anɔpa sԑ woba wo daadaa nneyɔeԑ mu a.
Sԑ wowɔ kuro kԑseԑ a nkurɔfoɔ nom anodeԑ ahodoɔ wɔ hɔ a, kɔ baabi a wɔtɔn bi wɔ wo mpɔtam hɔ a wontaa nkɔ hɔ.
Wɔn a wɔnnim nsԑmfua a adɔkotafoɔ de di dwuma mu no, nsԑmfua ‘infectious’ ԑne ‘contagious’ nkyerԑaseԑ nyԑ pԑ.
Sԑ yԑka sԑ yareԑ bi yԑ ‘infectious’ a, ԑyԑ yareԑ a ‘pathogen’ bi te sԑ ‘virus, bacterium, fungus’ anaa mmoawammoawa nkaeԑ bi na ԑde ba.
Sԑ yԑka sԑ yareԑ bi sae a, ԑyԑ yareԑ a wotumi nya bi wɔ berԑ a woabԑne obi a ɔwɔ bi.
Aban bebree hwԑ sԑ ahɔhoɔ a wɔreba ne man mu ԑne te man mufoɔ a wɔrefiri hɔ no bԑwɔ panneԑ wɔ nyarewa bi ho.
Deԑ ԑsԑ sԑ ɔkwantuni bi yԑ no gyina ɔman a wakɔ so anaa ɔpԑ sԑ ɔkɔ so no so.
Adeԑ a ԑdi tintim man ma Charlotte, North Carolina, ne sԑ ԑwɔ baabi pa bebree ma mmusua.
Nkurɔfoɔ a wɔfiri baabi foforɔ kyerԑ sԑ abusua nnamfofa ne adeԑ titire nti na wɔkɔ hɔ, ԑnna akwantufoɔ a mmɔfra ka wɔn ho ani gye wɔ kuro no mu.
Mfeԑ 20 a atwam no, mmɔfra nnamfofa akɔ soro wɔ Uptown Charlotte pa ara.
Abusua a wɔwɔ Charlotte ntaa mforo taxi, ԑwom sԑ ԑtaa boa wɔ kwan bi so.
Sԑ wɔfa akwantufoɔ a wɔn dodoɔ boro mmienu a, wɔgye sika no bi ka ho nti saa kwan yi boɔ bԑyԑ den asene sԑdeԑ ԑteԑ no.
Antartica ne beaeɛ a ɛhɔ yɛ nwunu pa ara wɔ asaase yi so, na atwa South Pole no ho ahyia.
Nsrahwɛ akwantuo boɔ yɛ den sane ɛhia ahoɔden, na ɛtumi di mu wɔ Obubuo de kɔsi Ɔgyefoɔ bosome a ɛyɛ ɔpɛ berɛ mu, na ɛgyina Peninsula, Islands ne Ross Sea so nko ara.
Adwumayɛfoɔ ahodoɔ bɛyɛ apem na wɔtena ha wɔ ɔpɛ berɛ mu wɔ mmeaeɛ ahodoɔ mu; nnipa no mu fa kumaa bi na wɔtena ha kɔsi nsutɔberɛ mu.
Inland Antarctica yɛ baabi a obiara nteɛ na asukɔtwea afa asaase no ani bɛyɛ kwasini mmienu anaa mmiɛnsa.
Ewiem nsrahwɛfoɔ a wɔba nsrahwɛ dapɔnna no kɔ asaase pradadaa so, sɛ wɔkɔ mmepɔ so anaa sɛ wɔbɛduru akɔnkɔ so a, wɔhwɛ nea aseɛ no trɛ.
South Pole Traverse no (anaa Highway) yԑ 1600 km ԑfiri McMurdo Station a ԑwɔ Ross Ɛpo no ho kɔsi Pole no.
Sukyerԑma no sԑdeԑ ayԑ no ԑnna wɔde frankaa ahyԑ no nso. Tractor soronko, ‘hauling sleds’ a fango wom na nneԑma wom na ԑbԑtumi afa mu.
Wɔtumi mfa mu ntԑm nti ԑsԑ sԑ ‘trail’ no kɔfa Transantarctic Mmepɔ no ho de ba asasetamaa no ho.
Deԑ ԑde akwanhyia ba wɔ osutɔ berԑ mu ne kwan a ԑso yԑ toro, baabi a wɔfa (kwan nkyԑn a wɔfa) ԑne ne titire ‘steps’.
Woannya koraa no, wohia mpaboa a aseԑ nyԑ toro. Mpaboa a wɔhyԑ no ɔpԑ berԑ no ase taa yԑ toro wɔ ‘ice’ ne sukyerԑma mu, osutɔ berԑ mu mpaboa bi koraa mmoa.
Ɛsԑ sԑ ԑmu dɔ sԑdeԑ ԑsԑ, 5 mm (1/5 inch) anaa deԑ ԑboro saa, na adeԑ a wɔde ayԑ no nso yԑ mmrԑ sԑdeԑ ԑsԑ wɔ awɔ berԑ mu.
Mpaboa no bi wɔ hɔ a ԑwɔ nnadeԑ wɔ aseԑ ԑnna yԑwɔ adeԑ a dadeԑ wɔ ho a ԑyԑ ma torotoro a mpaboa bebree bԑtumi de adi dwuma, a yԑde ma mpaboa a ԑtoɔ ware anaa nan no.
Ɛsԑ sԑ mpaboa to no wɔ fam na ԑyԑ tԑtrԑtԑ. Wɔtaa de anwea, abosea anaa nkyene (calcium chloride) pete kwan no mu sԑdeԑ ԑbԑyԑ a mpaboa no bԑkye.
‘Avalanches’ nkyerԑ sԑ nyԑ; bepɔ no baabi a apagya no tumi gye no kakra, na deԑ ԑbԑboro so no aba fam sԑ ‘avalanches’.
Ɔhaw no ne sԑ sukyerԑma kye adeԑ, ԑno nti ԑhia mpia bi ansa na aba fam ԑnna sukyerԑma no bi a ԑreba fam no bԑtumi apia deԑ ԑwɔ hɔ dada.
Ɛtɔ da a, deԑ ԑpia no ne awia a ԑrebɔ ma sukyerԑma no mu ayԑ hye no, ԑtɔ da a sukyerԑma a ԑretɔ no, ԑtɔ da a biribi foforɔ a ԑfiri abɔdeԑ nkaeԑ no ԑnna ԑtɔ da a ԑyԑ nnipa.
Mmotia mframa yԑ mframa a ԑretware ne ho a ԑtwe mframa no kɔ mu na ԑde no kɔ soro.
Wɔyԑ mframa no tenten a ano yԑ den (mpԑn pii ԑyԑ 100-200 miles/hour) na ԑbԑtumi apagya nneԑma a ԑmu yԑ duru akɔ wiem, na ԑde no kɔ baabi a mframa no bԑkɔ biara.
Ɛhyԑ aseԑ feaa te sԑ tokuro na ԑfiri soro asiane fam na adane "mmotia mframa" no.
Wɔn a wɔma ‘Personal VPN (virtual private network)’ yԑ kwan papa a wɔfa so de si amannyɔfoɔ kwan bɔne a wɔde nsԑntwerԑfoɔ fa so ԑne ‘commercial IP-geofiltering’ ano kwan.
Wɔn nimdeԑ fa ‘web proxies’ ho wɔ soro ԑnam nneԑma bebree nti: Wɔtumi dane Intanԑte so dwumadie nyinaa ani, na ԑnyԑ http nko ara.
Wɔtaa ma ‘bandwidth’ a ԑwɔ soro ԑne ɔsom a ԑwɔ soro. Wɔasɔ ano nti obi ntumi ntetԑ wo.
Nsԑntwerԑ dwuma no twa ntorɔ da biara fa dwumadie yi ho, wɔkyerԑ sԑ "wɔde resi kwan a wɔfa nkurɔfoɔ nimdeԑ" no ano kwan.
Nokorԑ no ne sԑ, mantam mmara nni nsunsuansoɔ wɔ sԑ woretwe obi adeԑ a etia mmara so; ‘disk’ a woatwe no nkakrankakra bԑtumi abɔ wɔ afidie biara a deԑ ԑyԑ papa no bԑtumi abɔ wɔ so biara.
Deԑ nti titire ne sԑ wɔbԑma saa nnwumakuo no tumi wɔ wɔn dwadie no so; ne nyinaa yԑ sika a ԑrekɔ ntwaaho.
Ɛnam sԑ wotumi frԑ wɔ Intanԑte so no nti, wonhia sԑ wode adwumamu fon a ԑwɔ wo mpɔtam no anaa baabi a wotu kwan kɔ no bԑdi dwuma.
Biribiara nso nni hɔ sԑ ԑsԑ sԑ wonya nɔma firi mpɔtam a wote no; wobԑtumi anya ‘satellite’ Intanԑte a wode bԑdi dwuma wɔ ‘wilds of Chicken, Alaska’ na woafa nɔma bi a ԑbԑkyerԑ sԑ wowɔ ‘sunny Arizona’.
Ɛtɔ da a wobԑhia sԑ wotɔ ‘wiase nɔma’ bi a ԑbԑma PSTN fon afrԑ wo. Baabi a nɔma no firi na ԑkyerԑ nnipa a wɔrefrԑ wo no nsonsonoeԑ.
‘Real-time text translator apps’ – yԑ ‘applications’ a ԑtumi kyerԑ kasa bi mu nsԑm ase de kɔ kasa foforɔ mu.
‘Applications’ a ԑwɔ saa kuo yi mu binom bԑtumi akyerԑ nsԑm a ԑwɔ kasa foforɔ mu a ԑfa nsԑnkyerԑnneԑ ho anaa nneԑma bi a ԑwɔ wiase yi mu ase sԑ deԑ ɔkuta ‘smartphone’ no de hwԑ adekorɔ no so a.
Nkyerԑaseԑ afidie ayԑ yie pa ara, nti seesei ԑma wo nkyerԑaseԑ a ԑyԑ papa (kakra bi na ԑyԑ nwura), nanso ahwԑyie kakra wɔ ho, ԑfiri sԑ ebia na ne nyinaa nyԑ papa.
Saa ‘apps’ a ԑwɔ saa kuo yi mu a agye din pa ara ne Google Translate, ԑyԑ a ԑma kwan ma wotumi yԑ nkyerԑaseԑ a ‘wo data nsi so’ berԑ a wɔatwe kasa korɔ no ‘data’ no awie no.
Sԑ wode ‘GPS navigation apps’ redi dwuma wɔ wo ‘smartphone’ so no yԑ kwan pa a wobԑtumi anante wɔ berԑ a wonni wo man mu.
Ɛbԑtumi ama woasie sika ԑfiri sԑ wontɔ ‘map’ foforɔ mma GPS bi, anaa ‘GPS afidie biara’ anaa wonhan bi mfiri wɔn a wɔde kaa ma ahan no hɔ.
Sԑ wonni ‘data’ wɔ wo fon no so anaa wonni baabi a ԑyԑ adwuma yie a, ne dwumadie so bԑte anaa ԑntumi nni dwuma koraa.
Fon kaade a wɔde tɔ ‘credit’ gu fon so bebree ahyԑ mantwea sotɔɔ biara mu ma a wobԑtumi de ama fon anaa tetefon yi ara.
Berԑ a kaade no bi yԑ ma ɔfrԑ wɔ baabiara no, ebinom yԑ dwuma soronko ma wotumi frԑ aman bi nko ara.
Saa dwuma yi ho akwannya taa nam tetefon nɔma a wofrԑ a wontua ka so.
Mmara a ԑfa mfonin twa ho nso kɔ ma sini twa nso, ԑkɔ ma no pa ara.
Sԑ woretwa biribi mfonin na ԑtia mmara a, ԑnneԑ mԑnnwene koraa sԑ wobԑtwa no sini.
Sԑ wode ‘drone’ redi dwuma a, hwԑ hunu deԑ mmara ma ho kwan sԑ wotwa ԑne deԑ wohia tumi krataa ansa na woatumi atwa.
Sԑ wode ‘drone’ bԑfa wiemhyԑn gyinabea anaa nnipadɔm so no nyԑ sԑ mpo ԑntia mmara wɔ baabi a wowɔ no a.
Nansa yi akwantuo a wɔfa wiem no, wɔntaa nyԑ wiemhyԑn no ho nhyehyԑeԑ wɔ berԑ a wɔnhwehwԑ ho asԑm na wɔmfa ԑboɔ no ntoto ho.
Ɛtɔ da a, wiemhyԑn baako no ara bԑtumi anya boɔ a ԑnyԑ pԑ nti ԑhia sԑ wode boɔ no bԑtoto ho na afei no wobԑhwԑ wiemhyԑn no ankasa wԑbsate no so ansa na woatɔ wo tikiti.
Ɛwom sԑ ebia wopԑ sԑ wokɔ akwansra anaa wokɔyԑ adwuma bi wɔ aman binom so a, wonhia visa nanso sԑ worekɔ a sԑ osuani no, wokyԑre hɔ sene sԑ worekɔ akwansra kԑkԑ.
Ne nyinaa ne sԑ, sԑ woretena ɔman foforɔ so berԑ tenten bi mu no, wohia sԑ wogye visa kane ansa.
Nneԑma a wɔhia ne kwan a wɔfa so nya asuafoɔ ‘visa’ ԑne kwan a wɔfa so nya akwansrafoɔ anaa wɔn a wɔrekɔyԑ adwuma bi ‘visa’ nyԑ pԑ.
Aman bebree wɔ hɔ a, wohia krataa a ԑfiri suapɔn no a wopԑ sԑ wokɔsua adeԑ wom no hɔ, ԑne wo sikasԑm ho adansedie sԑ sԑ wokɔ a wobԑtumi ahwԑ wo ho wɔ afe a ԑdi kan wɔ w’adesua no mu.
Hwehwԑ firi suapɔn no ԑne wɔn a wɔhwԑ akwantuo nsԑm so wɔ ɔman a wopԑ sԑ wokɔsua adeԑ wɔ mu no hɔ na gye nkyerԑmu.
Agye sԑ woyԑ aban ananmusini, ԑnte saa a, woreyԑ adwuma wɔ ɔman foforɔ so no kyerԑ sԑ ԑsԑ sԑ wotua ԑtoɔ ma ɔman no a wote mu no.
Ɛtoɔ tua ho nhyehyԑeԑ sesa wɔ aman ahodoɔ so, ԑnna ԑtoɔ dodoɔ a obi tua ԑne nnipa a wɔtua toɔ no sesa wɔ aman foforɔ so.
Aman a ԑwɔ nkyekyԑmu te sԑ United States ԑne Canada no, wɔgye toɔ no wɔ ɔman no ne mpɔtam hɔ no mmienu nti ԑtoɔ no ne nnipa a wɔtua no sesa firi mantam bi kɔ mantam bi mu.
Berԑ a wɔn a wɔhwԑ akwantufoɔ no nsi anaa bԑyԑ mmrԑ wɔ berԑ a woaduru wo man mu no, baabi a woyi nneԑma no deԑ ԑbԑtumi ama woabrԑ.
Hunu deԑ wobԑtumi de aba ne deԑ wontumi mfa mma na ka biribiara a ԑwom kyerԑ wɔn wɔ tumi krataa no so.
Kwan tiawa a wobԑfa so ahyԑ aseԑ wɔ ‘akwantuo mu atwerԑ’ dwumadie mu ne sԑ wobԑpԑ nimdeԑ wɔ ‘akwantuo blog’ wԑbsate bi a agye din so.
Berԑ a woahunu kwan a wɔfa so sesa nneԑma wɔ wԑb so no, afei akyire yi, wo nso bԑtumi ayԑ w’ankasa wo wԑbsate.
Sԑ wode wo ho bԑhyԑ dwumadie bi mu wɔ berԑ a woretu kwan ma woda nso nanso ԑnyԑ ɔma nko ara.
Sԑ wobԑtena na woayԑ dwumadie bi wɔ ɔman foforɔ so yԑ kwan kԑseԑ a wobԑtumi afa so ahunu amammerԑ foforɔ, ahyia nnipa foforɔ, ahu wo ho yie, ahunu kwan foforɔ a wɔfa so hwԑ biribi na woanya nimdeԑ foforɔ.
Ɛbԑtumi nso ayԑ kwan a wobԑfa so atwe wo sikasԑm mu na ama woatena baabi akyԑre ԑfiri sԑ saa adwuma no bebree ma wonya baabi da na kakra bi nso tua sika kakra ma wo.
‘Vikings’ faa Russian nsuo no so na ԑkɔɔ Black Sea ԑne Caspian Sea. Saa kwan yi baabi wɔ hɔ a, wobԑtumi afa so seesei. Hwԑ sԑ wobԑnya tumi krataa, a ԑyԑ den sԑ wo nsa bԑka.
White Sea–Baltic Canal no fa Arctic Ocean no mu kɔ Baltic Sea, nam Lake Onega so, Lake Ladoga ԑne Saint Petersburg, mpԑn pii nam asubɔntene ne asutadeԑ so.
Lake Onega sane nso bɔ Volga mu, ԑno nti sԑ wofiri Caspian Sea ԑrefa Russia no bԑtumi ayԑ yie.
Hyԑ no nso sԑ berԑ a wobԑduru suhyԑn gyinabea no ara biribiara bԑyԑ fann. Wobԑhyia suhyԑn foforɔ ԑmufoɔ no bԑka wɔn nsԑm akyerԑ wo.
Deԑ wobԑyԑ koraa ne sԑ wobԑboa abɔ nkurɔfoɔ nkaeԑ, nam baabi a suhyԑn gyina no ho, worekɔ nkurɔfoɔ a wɔrepopa wɔn suhyԑn ho, wo ne wɔn a wɔtwi suhyԑn no redi nkutaho ne ade.
Hwԑ sԑ wo ne nkurɔfoɔ bebree bԑkasa sԑdeԑ wobԑtumi. Ɛyԑ kakra a, obiara bԑhu wo na wɔakyerԑ wo suhyԑn a ԑrepԑ obi.
Ɛsԑ sԑ wofa ‘Frequent Flyer’ wiemhyԑn wɔ ‘alliance’ yie.
Ebia na ԑyԑ w’adwene sԑ ԑyԑ sԑ wobԑforo wiemhyԑn a daa wode tu kwan no ara, ԑsԑ sԑ wohunu sԑ akwannya a wɔde ma no taa sesa na ‘frequent flyer’ beaeԑ no bԑtumi ate so wɔ wiemhyԑn foforɔ wɔ saa ‘alliance’ hɔ ara.
Wiemhyԑn bi te sԑ Emirates, Etihad Airways, Qatar Airways & Turkish Airlines abae wɔ dwumadie mu akɔ Abibiman mu, na wɔdi dwuma wɔ Abibiman nkuropɔn titire bebree mu wɔ boɔ a ԑwɔ fam sene European wiemhyԑn nkaeԑ no.
Turkish Airlines kɔ baabi 39 wɔ Abibiman man 30 ԑfiri afe 2014.
Sԑ wowɔ berԑ kakra a, hwehwԑ sika a wobԑtua akɔ Abibiman mu no na fa toto deԑ wotua de kɔ wiase baabi foforɔ no ho.
Ɛmma wo werԑ mfiri sԑ wobԑfa sika a wode bԑtua visa foforɔ ka, ԑtoɔ a wotua sԑ worefiri hɔ a, sika a wode bԑfa kaa ne ade ma saa beaeԑ a ԑnni Abibiman mu no.
Sɛ wopɛ sɛ wotu kwan fa wiase nyinaa wɔ Anaafoɔfam Ntwahohyiafa no mu a, ɔhye da ewiemuhyɛn mu akwantuo ne mmeaɛ a wo bɛkɔ no ho esiane ɔkwan a enni ɛpo no so no nti.
Ewiemuhyɛn adwumakuo nkabom biara nni hɔ a ɛkata ɛpo so ntwamu kwan mmiɛnsa a ɛwɔ Anaafoɔfam Ntwahihyiafa no nyinaa so (na SkyTeam nkata ntwamu kwan no mu biara so).
Ɛmfa ho no, Star Alliance kata biribiara so agye apueɛfam Anaafoɔ Pacific no afiri Santiago de Chile de kosi Tahiti, a ɛyɛ LATAM Oneworld ewiemuhyɛn mu akwantuo.
Nnyɛ saa ewiemuhyɛn mu akwantuo wei nkoaa na wobetumi apa sɛ wopɛ sɛ wo bɔ tra Anaafoɔ Pacific no ne Anaafoɔ America atɔeɛ mpoano no a. (hwɛ aseɛ hɔ)
Wɔ 1994 mu no, Armenian Nagorno-Karabakh abusukuo a afi Azerbaijan no tuu ɔko so sa tiaa Azeris.
Wɔ tee akwasafoɔman foforɔ aberɛ a na Armeniafoɔ bɔ akyidɔm no. Nanso, ɔman a wɔn ate biara - mpo Armenia no - nnim.

Wɔde UNESCO Wiase Amammerɛ Beaɛ dwumadie ahyɛ mansni no nyinaa nsa esiane n'amammerɛ ne n'abakɔsɛm a ɛyɛ soronko na ɛsombo no, na n'agyapadeɛ a ɛsom bo no ka deɛ ɛwowɔ soro paa wɔ ɔman no mu no ho.
Nkura nketewa anum a ɛno ne Riomaggiore, Manarola, Corniglia, Vernazza ne Monterosso na ɛka bom yɛ Cinque Terre, a asekyerɛ ne Nsase Anum, ɛwɔ Italy mantam mu wɔ Liguria.

Mfe ɔpepem a atwam no, nkurɔfoɔ de ahwɛyie asisi terraces wɔ asase hutuhutu, a agyina hɔ kuronkuron wɔ abotan no so a ɛma ɛpo no yɛ fɛ.
Ɔfa bi a ɛkyere adwene a ɛka ho no yɛ mpuntuo nkabom a wɔnni no. Anammɔnkwan, keteke ne kodoɔ ka nkura no bom, na ahyɛn entumi ndu hɔ firi abɔnten.
French kasa ahodoɔ a wɔka wɔ Belgium ne Switzerland no nsonsonoeɛ kakra wɔ mu sen French a wɔka wɔ France no, nanso nsɛdie wɔ mu a ɛma no yɛ mmerɛ sɛ wobɛte aseɛ.
Titire no, wɔ akontahyɛdeɛ mu wɔ Belgium ne Switzerland a wɔka French no adeɛ soronko kakra wɔ ho a ɛda nso firi French a wɔ ka wɔ France no, na nsonsonoeɛ kakra da sɛdeɛ wɔ bɔ nsɛmfua bi ntam.
Nanso, nanka ɛsɛ sɛ Belgiumfoɔ ne Swissfoɔ a wɔka French no sua French ɔfranka wɔ sukuu mu, sɛdeɛ ɛbɛyɛ a anka wɔ bɛte w'ase sɛ mpo wode French ɔfranka akontahyɛdeɛ de dwuma a.
Wɔ wiase no afa bebree mu no, wo nsa a wobɛ him no yɛ ayɔnkofa suo, a ɛkyerɛ "hello."
Nanso, wɔ Malaysia, wɔ Malays a wɔwɔ nkura aseɛ no mu no, ɛkyerɛ "bra ha,", tesɛ akyerɛkyerɛ kwan nsatea a wɔ bu ba nipadua no anim no, honam yɛbeaɛ a wɔ de di dwuma wɔ Atɔeɛfam aman pii so, na saa atrimpɔ no nkoaa nti na ɛsɛ sɛ wo de di dwuma sa.
Saa ara nso na, British ɔkwantufoɔ a ɔwɔ Spain bɛ susu sɛ nsa a wɔ him a nsa yam no kyerɛ nipa a ɔrehim ne nsa de adi nkra no (mmom sen nipa a wo him wo nsa akyerɛ no) sɛ yɛbeaɛ a ɛkyerɛ sɛ san w'akyi bra.
Kasa ahodoɔ a ɛboa ɛyɛ kasa a nkurɔfoɔ ayɛ anaa kasa a wɔn ahyehyɛ a wɔ yɛeɛ sɛ ɛbɛ boa nkɔmɔbɔ wɔ nkurɔfoɔ a nkɔmɔbɔ ho yɛ den ma wɔ no ntam.

Wɔ ɔhyew mu wɔ da no mu no, akwantufoɔ betumi ahu anisoadehunu a ɛfa nsuo ho (anaasɛ nneɛma afoforɔ).
Weinom betumi ayɛ hu sɛ ɔkwantufoɔ no toa n'anisoadehu no so a, ɛsɛe ahoɔden a ɛsombo ne nsuo a aka.
Ɛserɛ so a ɛso yɛ hye paa mpo no betumi abɛyɛ nwunu paa wɔ anadwo. Hypothermia yɛ asiane ankasa sɛ wonni ntadeɛ a ɔhyew wɔ mu a.
Wɔ ahuhuroberɛ mu, titire no, ɛsɛ sɛ wohwɛ ntomtom kwan sɛ wosi gyinaeɛ sɛ wobɛ nante kwaeɛ no mu de agyegye w'ani a.

Nnomaa yareɛ, anaasɛ nea na wɔferɛ no avian influenza no, betumi aka nnomaa ne nufuboa nyinaa.

Adeɛ tiitire ma Norway no yɛ fjords ntɛmtɛm ne amena a mpofirimu no ɛma kwan a ɛwɔ soro, bɛyɛ asase kɛseɛ mpagyamu a ɛwɔ soro.
Asase kɛseɛ mpagyamu a ɛwɔ soro yi tae kyerɛ "vidde" asekyerɛ ne deɛ ɛtrɛ, kwan a dua biara nni, asasetam a ɛnni akwansideɛ biara.

Nsukyene akɛseɛ no ɛnyɛ pintin, nanso ɛsen fa bepɔw no ase. Wei bɛma mpaeɛ, tokuro, a abia nsuokyerɛma no mu no de bɛ ahinta no.
Nsuokyene amoa nkatasoɔ ne aban betumi adwiri na mpaeɛ betumi asi.
Wɔ nsuokyene akɛseɛ ano no nsuokyene kuntann bubu yɛ nketewa, wɔgu fam na ebia wɔ huru anaasɛ wɔ muni firi ano kɔ akyire.

Nanso, wɔwɔ ahoɔfɛ ne kaberɛ a ɛyɛ soronko wɔ awɔ berɛ mu, ne mmepɔw gyinabea bebree a wɔgye nsukyerɛma dodoɔ a ɛte apɔw na ɛma dwumadie te sɛ nsukyerɛma so agorɔdie ne snowboarding kɔ so.
Ewiemhyɛn adwumakuo kakraa bi pɛ na wɔ daso ma wɔn a wɔn ahwere wɔn adɔfo nkwa ho akwanneɛ, a ɛte akwantuo mu ayie yɛ ho aka no so kakraa bi.
Ewiemhyɛn adwumakuo a wɔ ma wei bi ne Canada ewiemhyɛn adwumakuo, Delta ewiemhyɛn adwumakuo, Lufthansa ma wim akwantuo a ɛfiri U.S anaasɛ Canada, ne WestJet.
