Mpↄtam hↄ foↄ no abufuo no ama wↄrebↄ mmↄden seesei sɛ wↄbɛyɛ nhyehyeɛ afa ↄbarima ne ↄbaa nna ho nsɛm ma saet no a ɛgye dawurobↄ nwuma a wↄwↄ hokwan ↄpepem pii a wↄde wↄn nsɛm bɛto hↄ no.
Adwuma a wↄyɛe no fa kɛseɛ no ara yɛ nhwehwɛmu ne nkyerɛkyerɛmu, nanso wↄyɛɛ dwumadie no ho twerɛtohↄ sɛdeɛ ɛne deɛ wↄhyɛɛ no nsow wↄ Sagittarius nsoroma kuo no mu no bedi nsɛ.
Nsunsuansoↄ a tumi a ɛma nsoromma kuo no" dark matter" ne "Milky Way dark matter" no keka wↄn ho no de ba no na ekuo no rehwɛ kwan sɛ ebesi.
Sɛdeɛ ↄsram no tumi twe asase no, na ɛma asorↄkye si no, sa ara nso na Milky Way no tumi twe Sagittarius nsorommakuo no.
Abↄdeɛ mu nyanasahunufo tumi ka sii so sɛ "dark matter" nya 'dark matter" foforo so tumi na saa ara nso na "regular matter" nso teɛ.

Onipa a ɔgyee sikakɔkɔɔ abasobɔdeɛ kɛseɛ pa ara no nyaa saa abasobɔdeɛ no ɛnam 100m ne 200m nsuomudware akansie a wɔde kyerɛ bɔberɛ, ne nnadaaho mmiɛnsa a wɔyɛ no wɔ Commonwealth Agokansie mu, nanso ɛnam nkuro a ɔbɔɔeɛ no nti ama n’apomden no atɔ kyima kakra.
Ɔntumi mfa nnuro a ɛho hia sɛ ɛboa ma ne yaw no korɔ no esiane sɛ wabra wɔ agokansie no mu.
Curtis Cooper a ɔkyerɛ nkontabuo ne kɔmputa abɔdeɛ mu nyansapɛ wɔ University of Central Missouri, ahunu ‘prime’ nɔma a ɛso pa ara bɛsi nnɛ wɔ Ɔpɛpɔn 25 mu.
Nnipa bebree nam kɔmputa nkorabata a yɛtumi sɔ mu ne nea yɛntumi nsɔ mu so de sii n’adehunu no so dua wɔ Ɔgyefoɔ bosome ahyɛaseɛ na wɔbɔɔ ho dawuro Benada.
Wɔgye di sɛ ‘Comet’ na ɛnam so ma nsuo ba asase so, na ɛne adeɛ bi a ɛtumi ma yɛ nnipa dua mu ahoɔden na ɛbɔ nkwa ho ban na ɛdi dwuma bom.
Abɔdeɛ mu nhwehwɛmufoɔ pɛsɛ wɔhunu ɔkwan a akyinsoromma ba, nkanka sɛnea ewiase baeɛ, esianesɛ ‘comets’ taa ne asase hyia firi mmere santen.
Cuomo, 53, hyɛɛ ne mampanin dwumadie ase afe yi ahyɛaseɛ na wadane mmara bi adi bosome a atwam a ɛkyerɛ sɛ mmarima anaa mmaa mmienu bɛtumi aware.
Ɔkaa sɛ saa atesɛm no yɛ "amanyɔ nsɛnkeka ne nsɛmhunu".
Yɛretete no mframa mu sɛ ɔpɛ sɛ ɔbɛyɛ mampanin wɔ afe 2016 mu.
NextGens yɛ adeɛ bi a FFA reka sɛ ɛbɛboa ama wiemhyɛn atu afa mmea a wɔtoto atuo na akɔ agye fangoo ɔpepe afe biara afiri ɔsɛeɛ mu na asane nso ate mframa bɔne a ɛsɛe mframa pa so.
Ɛde mfididwuma mu nkɔanim sɛtelaite na ɛdi dwuma na mmom ɛnyɛ tete kwan so a na wɔde mfididwuma mu nkɔanim a na ɛnam fɔm di dwuma no, sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ ɛbɛma mfidie a ɛhwɛ wiemhyɛn dwumadie so wɔ wiem atumi ayɛ n’adwuma fann na ama wiemhyɛnkafoɔ nsɛm korɔgyee a mfomsoɔ biara nni ho.
Wɔmfaa beaeɛ a ɛbɛgyina nea ɛtɔ so nkaa ho, na keteke a ɛnam asase ase nso nnyina wɔ Wembley, na kaa nnyina na afei nso yɛnnya baabi a yɛde kaa bɛsisi wɔ beaeɛ hɔ.
Ɔhu a na ɛtaa akyire sɛ nnipa nnya kaa mforo no maa sɛ wɔreyɛ akansie kokoam no maa ne ho mene so a akyitaafoɔ nka ho.
Adesuadeɛ bi a wɔdaa no adi Yawoada no wɔ koowaa krataa a ɛfa abɔdeɛ mu nyansapɔ mu daa no adi sɛ nnomaa foforɔ bi apue mu wɔ Ecuadorean Galápagos Islands.
Adeusa nhwehwɛmufoɔ a wɔfiri Princeton University a ɛwɔ Amɛrika ne Uppsala University a ɛwɔ Sweden kaa sɛ saa nnomaa foforɔ pueeɛ bɛyɛ mfeɛ kakra akyi, mmom wɔgye di sɛ saa nsusuiɛ no akyɛ kakra deɛ, ɛnam mmoawa Darwin finch, Geospiza fortes, aboawa cactus finch a wabɛfra mu ne Geospiza conirostris awoɔ nnidisoɔ.
Wobɛtumi asesa sika kɔkɔɔ afaafa ahodoɔ pii. Wobɛtumi nso asese no ayɛ no nketenkete.
Wobɛtumi adane no ama ayɛ sɛ ahoma, a yɛbɛtumi akoa mu nea yɛpɛ. Yɛbɛtumi abobɔ so anaa abaebae mu ama ayɛ traa.
Yɛbɛtumi ama no ayɛ traa ama atare dadeɛ afoforɔ so. Yɛtumi yɛ no tea pa ara ma ɔtɔ da koraa a yɛtumi de siesie mfonii a yɛde yɛn nsa ayɛ wɔ nwoma bi mu a yɛfrɛ no "nwoma yɛn ankasa ayɛ a ɛte yerɛyerɛw".
Wei na wɔfrɛ no ‘chemical pH’ no. Wobɛtumi ayɛ adeɛ a ɛda biribi adi wɔ berɛ a wode ‘red cabbage juice’ reyɛ.
‘Cabbage juice’ no sesa n’ahosuo de kyerɛ sɛ adeɛ no ‘acidic’ anaa ‘basic’ (alkaline).
‘Hydrogen ions’ dodoɔ a ɛwɔ adeɛ no mu na ɛkyerɛ ne ‘pH level’ (the H in pH).
‘Hydrogen ions’ yɛ ‘protons’ are wɔahwere wɔn ‘electrons’ (esiane sɛ ‘Hydrogen atoms’ kura ‘Proton baako ne ‘electron’ baako).
Nu paada a a woɔ no mmienu bom na afei, fa nsa a ɛho awoɔ bobɔ no kurukuruwa.
Nsuo kakra a ɛwɔ wo nsa ho no ne adeɛ no akyi bɛdi ahyia, na ama no asesa kakra na adane biribi tesɛ abena.
Na nkuro bi te sɛ Harappa and Mohenjo-daro wɔ abɛɛfo tiefi wɔ afie biara mu a na wɔde mmɔnka pepeafo nso aka ho.
Yɛda so hunu mmɔnka yi ho adeɛ binom wɔ afie ahodoɔ mu wɔ Minoan nkuro a ɛwɔ Crete ne Santorini a ɛwɔ Greece.
Na tete mmerɛ mu Egypt, Persia ne Chinafoɔ nso wɔ tiefi wɔ wɔn afie mu. Wɔ Roman anibue berɛ mu no, na wɔtaa de tiefi hyɛ adwareeɛ ma mmaa ne mmarima nyinaa tu fra kɔ mu.
Sɛ wofrɛ obi a wo ne ne ntam kwan ware bɛyɛ kwansini mpem a, na wode ‘satellite’ na ɛredi dwuma.
Saa ‘satellite’ yi a ɛwɔ wiem no di kan nya ɔfrɛ no na adane no aba asase so mpofirim.
Wɔde afidie a yɛde kɔ wiem na ɛde ‘satellite’ yi kɔɔ soro. Abɔdeɛ mu nyansapɛfoɔ de ‘telescope’ na ɛdi dwuma wɔ wiem ɛfiri sɛ wiem nsakraeɛ mma yɛnhunu nkanea ne ne hyerɛn yie.
Ansa na afidie a yɛde kɔ wiem a ɛso pa ara bɛtumi de ‘satellite’ anaa ‘telescope’ abɔ wiem no, ɛwɔ sɛ ɛkɔ soro bɛyɛ anmmɔn 100.
Kaa asesa nneɛma bebree wɔ wiase yi mu wɔ akwan pii so. Deɛ ɛsombo pa ara kaa ayɛ ne sɛ, ama yɛn akwantuo ayɛ mmrɛ asane nso ayɛ ntɛm.
Abrɛ yɛn keteke, kaa, ne mfidie ahodoɔ bebree a yɛde tu kwan.
Wɔn ase na mmoa a wɔwe mmoa foforɔ a wɔyԑ hɔ ne hɔ hyԑ na wɔwe mmoa hɔ ne hɔ bi te sԑ nnanko, atwe ne ɔforoteԑ.
Deԑ ԑtwa toɔ, yɛwɔ nnyinammoa nketewa (a afiboa a wɔnni hwɛsofoɔ ka ho) a wɔwe mmoa foforɔ nketewa pii wɔ hɔ a wɔwe mmoa nketewa bi te sԑ, nkoekoeboa, akuransԑsoɔ, nkoterԑ ne nnomaa.
Adeԑ a ԑma wɔkɔ so ne deԑ yԑfrԑ no ‘niche’ no, ԑyԑ adwumason a mmoa no mu biara die a ɔne afoforɔ mpere ho.
Gyata ne mmoa no mu deԑ wɔfa ayɔnkoɔ pa ara, wɔtena akuo bebree a yԑfrԑ no ‘prides’.
‘Prides’ no yԑ mmarima mpanimfoɔ no baako kɔsi mmiԑnsa a wɔbɔ abusua, na mmaa aduasa ne wɔn mma ka ho.
Mmaa no taa hwe bom ma wɔyԑ abusua kԑseԑ a wɔyԑ nnua mmaa ne mma mmaa.
Gyata ‘pride’ no yԑ adwuma te sԑ sakraman anaa nkraman a wɔte sԑ gyata (na mmom nyԑ mmoa akԑseԑ nkaeԑ no) wɔ suban mu, ԑnna wɔn ho yԑ hu ma mmoa a wɔkye wɔn no.
Ɔsebɔ bԑtumi aforo dua (nanso nyԑ pa ara), adware nsuom, ahuru kԑseԑ, ԑnna ɔwɔ ahoɔden kyԑn nnipa mprԑ nnum.
Ɔsebɔ ne gyata, kankane, ne ‘gyagua’ na wɔwɔ ekuo baako (Genus Panthera) mu. Saa mmoa nnan yi nko ara na wɔtumi bobom.
Ɔsebɔ mmobom no nte sԑ gyata deԑ kԑseԑ no na mmom ԑte sԑ deԑ ɔreyԑ ɔkasamu anaa ɔreka nsԑm bi no.
‘Ocelots’ taa we mmoa nketewa. Sԑ wɔbԑtumi a, wɔkye nnoe, awɔ, akuransԑsoɔ ԑne nnomaa. Mmoa a ‘ocelot’ kye wɔn no nyinaa yԑ nketewa sene no.
Abɔdeԑ mu nyansapԑfoɔ dwene sԑ ‘ocelot’ de pampan ne fam ahuahua (mmoa a wɔwe) na nya mmoa kye wɔn we.
Wɔhunu adeԑ anadwo pa ara ԑnna wɔnante wɔ kwan a afoforɔ nhu no nso so. Kwan a ‘ocelot’ fa so kye mmoa ne sԑ, wɔde wɔn ho fra baabi a wɔwɔ no na wɔato ahyԑ mmoa no so.
Sԑ nneԑma a nkwa wowɔ mu kuo ketewa bi (wɔn dodoɔ yԑ kakra bi) yera firi dodoɔ no a wɔfiri mu no a (te sԑ, sԑ wɔkɔfa mmepɔ bi so anaa asuo bi ho anaa wɔkɔ asase foforɔ a wɔntumi nsane wɔn akyi mma bio a) mpԑn pii baabi a wɔakɔduru no bԑdane baabi foforɔ ma wɔn.
Saa baabi foforɔ yi wɔ nneԑma ԑne wɔn a wɔne wɔn bԑpere ho foforɔ nti wɔbԑhia sԑ wɔdane wɔn ho foforɔ sԑdeԑ ԑbԑyԑ a wɔbԑtumi ne afoforɔ no apere sene sԑdeԑ na wɔyԑ no kane no.
Wɔn dodoɔ no nsesae koraa, wɔda so hia sԑdeԑ na wɔteԑ dada no ara.
Akyire yi sԑ ekuo foforɔ no hyԑ aseԑ hunu baabi foforɔ no tena a, wɔhyԑ aseԑ sԑ wɔresesa afiri ekuo dodoɔ no ho.
Afei, mfeԑ mpempem anaa ɔpepem akyire no, saa akuo yi mmienu sesa koraa a wontumi nka sԑ wɔyԑ baako.
Yԑfrԑ saa adeԑ yi ‘speciation’ a ԑkyerԑ sԑ wɔayԑ ekuo foforɔ. ‘Speciation’ yԑ adeԑ a wontumi nsi ano na ԑyԑ pa ara ma nnanemu anaa nsesa ba.
Nnua na wɔyԑ mframa a nnipa home no, na wɔagye mframa a nnipa home ba abɔntene no (ԑne sԑ, wɔhome ba abɔntene).
Nnua de awia nam ‘photosynthesis’ so noa wɔn aduane. Wɔsane nso ma nwunu.
Yԑde nnuasi yԑn fie sane nya ntadeԑ firi nnua mu. Nnuane ahodoɔ a yԑdie yԑ nnua. Sԑ nnua nni hɔ a, mmoa nnya nkwa.
Na Mosasaurus yɛ aboa kɛse tenten kyɛn aboa biara wɔ wɔn bere so, a no ɔtow hyɛ mmoa afoforo so. Na wɔnsuro hwee, gye mosasaurus ahoforo.
N'apantan tenten no wɔ ɛse bɛbro 70 a ɛyɛ nam sɛ blade. Ɛno akyi no, ɔwɔ ɛse fofro wɔ nanum soro hɔ, a aseɛ ne sɛ, biribiara ntumi ntwam wɔ n'anum a ebeguan.
Yentumi nsi no pi, nanso na ebia ɔwɔ tɛkrɛma a ɛte sɛ adinam. Na nnuan a odi no bi ne nsuo mu akyekyedeɛ, nsuo mu nnam akɛse, mosasaurus afoforo, ne ebia nnipa.
Ɔtow hyɛ biribiara a ɛbɔwura nsuo no mu no so; dinosaur kɛse tenten te sɛ T.rex mpo ntumi no.
Ɛwom sԑ yԑnim wɔn nnuane deԑ, nanso na Romanfoɔ wɔ nnuane bi a na ԑyԑ soronko anaa nwanwa bi te sԑ, ‘prakonini’, ‘peacock’, nwa, ԑne akuransԑsoɔ bi a yԑfrԑ no ‘dormouse’.
Nsonsonoeԑ baako bio ne sԑ, berԑ a ahiafoɔ ne mmaa tena akonnwa mu di wɔn aduane no, na asikafoɔ no taa yԑ ‘banquet’ pԑ baabi tena di wɔn aduane no.
‘Ancient Roman’ nnuane no nni nnuane a ԑfiri Amerika aba Europe anaa Asia bi wom wɔ mfeԑ ɔha a ԑtwa toɔ no mu.
Nhwԑsoɔ ne sԑ, na wɔnni aburo, anaa ntoosi, anaa abrɔfo ntɔmmԑ, anaa kookoo, ԑnna tete Romani biara nni hɔ a ɔde kurokurokoko kaa n’ano da.
Babelfoɔ no sii dan maa wɔn abosom no mu biara na ԑhɔ na wɔfa no sԑ ɔbosomkorɔ no wɔ.
Nkurɔfoɔ bԑbɔ afɔdeԑ ma saa abosom no ԑnna wɔn asomfoɔ no nso nam nnadie ne afahyԑ so yԑ wɔn ahiadeԑ ma wɔn.
Na beaeԑ no nyinaa wɔ baabi petee a nnipa no nyinaa tumi ba ԑnna kronkron mu bea a asomfoɔ no nko ara na wɔ kɔ hɔ.
Ɛtɔ da a wɔsi ‘pyramid’ abansoro soronko bi a wɔfrԑ no ‘ziggurats’ ka asɔredan ne ho.
Abansoro no soro yԑ baabi a soronko ma bosom no.
Sԑ ԑduru ahuhuro berԑ wɔ Middle East a, efie ho nhia bio.
Hebrew abusua no nneԑma bebree kɔ so wɔ petee mu.
Mmaa noa aduane wɔ adi hɔ, ‘stores’ no nso yԑ baabi a wɔbue wɔ kwan no ho. Na wɔde aboɔ si dan.
Na kwaeԑ akԑseԑ nni Canaan, nti na nnua boɔ yԑ den pa ara.
Na ‘Greenland’ atenaeԑ no ahwete. Wɔka wɔ ‘Norse sagas’ no mu sԑ wɔtwaa ‘Erik the Red’ asu firii Iceland sԑ wakum obi, nti berԑ a ɔde n’ani kyerԑԑ atɔeԑ no na ɔhunuu Greenland too ne din Greenland.
Nanso saa berԑ no a ɔhunuu saa beaeԑ foforɔ yi no, na Eskimo abusua no te hɔ dada.
Ɛwom sԑ na aman no nyinaa yԑ 'Scandinavian', nanso na nsonsonoeԑ bebree wɔ nnipa no, ahemfo, amanneԑ, ԑnne abakɔsԑm a ԑda Denmark, Sweden, Norway ԑnne Iceland ntam.
Sԑ woahwԑ sini a ԑde ‘National Treasure’ no a, wobԑdwene sԑ na wɔatwerԑ ‘treasure map’ wɔ Fawohodie a Wɔpaeԑ no akyi.
Nanso ԑnyԑ nokorԑ saa. Ɛwom sԑ wɔatwerԑ biribi wɔ nwoma no akyi deԑ nanso ԑnyԑ ‘treasure map’.
Nsԑm a na wɔatwerԑ agu Fawohodie krataa no akyi ne "Fawohodie Mpaemu no Ankasa, wɔ Kutawonsa 4 1776". Nsԑm a wɔatwerԑ no wɔ krataa no fam a asi ne tiri ase.
Berԑ a obiara nnim onipa a ɔtwerԑeԑ no, yԑnim sԑ wɔde saa nwoma kԑseԑ yi a (na esusu 29¾ inches by 24½ inches) siee baabi.
Wei nti, ԑbԑyԑ sԑ wɔde saa asԑm no too so sԑ ne din.
‘D-Day landings’ ԑne ntɔkwa a ԑtoaa so no maa France atifi fam dee ne ho, nanso na anaafoɔ fam deԑ ԑnnee ne ho.
Na "Vichy" French no na ԑdi so. Weinom yԑ Frenchfoɔ a na wɔne German ayԑ asomdwoeԑ apam wɔ afe 1940 mu na wɔne wɔn a wɔbԑtohyԑԑ wɔn so no nko na mmom wɔyԑ adwuma bom.
Ɔsanaa 15 1940, wɔn a wɔaka wɔn ho abom no wuraa France anaafoɔ hɔ, saa adeԑ no din de "Operation Dragoon".
Nnawɔtwe mmienu ntam na Amerikafoɔ ne Frence asogyafoɔ a wɔade wɔn ho no agye wɔn a wɔwɔ France anaafoɔ no ma wɔde wɔn ani akyerԑ German.
Anibue yԑ amanneԑ baako a nnipakuo bebree a wɔte bom na wɔyԑ adwuma bom, fekuo de di dwuma.
Asԑmfua ‘civilization’ firi ‘Latin civilis’ mu, ԑkyerԑ ‘civil’ a ԑne ‘Latin civis’ bɔ abusua, a ԑkyerԑ ‘citizen’, ԑne ‘civitas’, a ԑkyerԑ ‘city anaa city-state’, ԑnna ԑno nso tumi kyerԑ fekuo no kԑseԑ.
‘City-states’ no ara ne aman no. Anibue amanneԑ kyerԑ sԑ wɔrekyerԑ nkyirimma nimdeԑ bi ama awɔ hɔ daadaa na wɔde ama nkyirimma.
Amammerԑ nketewa bi tumi yera wɔ berԑ a ԑnnya abakɔsԑm biara wɔ hɔ nti wɔnhu sԑ ԑyԑ anibue papa.
‘Revolutionary War’ no berԑ mu no, ‘thirteen states’ no yԑԑ aban a emu yԑ mmrԑ bi—a ‘Congress’ no nko ara na na wɔyԑ saa aban no—wɔ ‘Articles of Confederation’ no ase.
Na ‘Congress’ no nni tumi biara sԑ ԑde ԑtoɔ bԑto nnipa no so, ԑnna ԑnam sԑ na ‘national executive anaa judiciary’ no nni hɔ nti, na ɔdan ‘state authorities’ no nso na wɔmmoa no.
Na ԑnni tumi biara sԑ ԑbԑyԑ biribi afa mmara a ԑda ԑtoɔ ho wɔ ‘states’ no ntam no ho.
Na ‘Articles’ no hia sԑ nnipa no nyinaa bԑgye atom ansa na wɔatumi asesa no nanso na ‘states’ no mfa ‘central government’ no nsԑm nyԑ asԑm biara nti na wɔn ananmusifoɔ no koraa kɔ hɔ.
‘Italy man no bɔɔlobɔ kuo, ԑne German man no bɔɔlobɔ kuo no yԑ bɔɔlobɔ kuo a ԑtɔ so mmienu a adi yie pa ara wɔ wiase akansie mu ԑnna wɔn na wɔgyee FIFA World Cup wɔ afe 2006 mu.
Agokansie a agye din bi te sԑ ‘football, basketball, volleyball, water-polo, fencing, rugby, cycling, ice hockey, roller hockey ԑne F1 motor racing’.
‘Winter sports’ no agye din wɔ Atifi fam, a Italy man no si akan wiase akansi ne Olympic dwumadie mu.

Adan a εwↄ adan a wↄn asi no woworane no ano no wↄn asan esi biom sεdeε εbεma nsrahwεfoↄ anya adan no teε ankasa.

Wↄdaso yε de bεsi nnε, nanso dea εho hia paa yε sεdeε εteε a mfonitwa afidie ho nkateε abεsi anan mu no.

Sεdeε εteε no (sε yεkyεmu dubaako na yenya akontahyεdeε a εno nkoaa gyina a) ma yεka sε εyε 3:2.
